Local News

Thirteenth Annual Hygiene Campaign Opens: Citywide Hygiene Lockdown for One Week; Representatives from Party, Government, and Military Participate in Light Rain; Mayor Wu and Bureau Chiefs Personally Sweep Streets 104

According to the Central News Agency, the opening ceremony of the Thirteenth Annual Hygiene Campaign of this city was held at the Daji Road Public Sports Field on the 19th at 10:30 AM. Despite the light rain, various agencies, organizations, and schools arrived at the sports field on time to participate. After speeches by Mayor Wu and the heads of various bureaus, they all personally took up brooms and swept the streets on Daji Road. Starting from the 19th, a citywide hygiene lockdown will be in effect for one week. Details are as follows:

Participants from Various Sectors 105

Those who participated in the ceremony included: Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Party Committee Tong Xingbai, Director of the Municipal Health Bureau Li Tingan, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau Wen Hongen, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau Xu Peihuang, Director of the Municipal Land Bureau Jin Liren (represented by Yang Nianzu), Representative of the Health Department of the International Settlement Allen, Representative of the Health Department of the French Concession Xu Chuanjun, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Wang Xiaolai, Huang Rende of the Chinese Medicine Association, Tu Kaizheng of the Pharmaceutical Industry Association,

Liu Xinde of the China Children's Welfare Association, Zhang Wei of the Chinese Medical Association, Zhang Junjun of the China Anti-Tuberculosis Association, Ling Xitao of the YMCA, Wei Zhenpei of the YWCA, as well as over a thousand representatives from the city's New Life Movement Persuasion Teams, schools, organizations, agencies, and all levels of Party headquarters.

Venue Setup 106

Inside the Public Sports Field, a podium was erected with a banner reading "Shanghai Thirteenth Annual Hygiene Campaign" above it. In the center of the stage, portraits of the Party, the nation, and Sun Yat-sen were hung. The recording seats were arranged on both sides, and the Public Security Bureau military band was present to participate. Various cloth banners with slogans such as "Pay Attention to Cleanliness," "Vigorously Promote Hygiene Campaign," and "Implement Thorough Cleaning" were hung throughout the venue. Hygiene posters were plastered all around, and over a hundred specially prepared brooms were available for people to use for cleaning.

Director Li's Report 107

After the ritual ceremony, Director Li Tingan, the chairman of the campaign, gave a report, briefly stating: The Twelfth Annual Hygiene Campaign of Shanghai will be opened today.

Opening Ceremony Speech by Mayor Wu (Xu Tianzhang) 108

I deeply recognize the importance of personal health, so we cannot ignore personal and public hygiene. This city holds a hygiene campaign every year. This time, it coincides with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's promotion of the New Life Movement, so this year's hygiene campaign has been further expanded. There are twenty or thirty participating groups and organizations, and I am very grateful for the enthusiastic assistance of the participating groups and organizations, which has made everything proceed smoothly. There are five things to pay attention to in this year's hygiene campaign: (1) Develop good habits for spitting; (2) Urinate in the toilet; (3) Throw garbage into the garbage can; (4) Drink boiled water; and (5) Get vaccinated. These five things are the most important. If all our citizens can do the above five things, then public hygiene will have better results.

Mayor's Speech 109

Next, Mayor Wu Tiecheng gave a speech, briefly stating that today is the opening of the city's thirteenth cleaning campaign. Cleaning is the basic work of public hygiene and can also be said to be an important condition for promoting public hygiene construction. There are many people in cities, and whether the urban population is healthy or not is closely related to the success or failure of the entire urban undertaking. We live in cities and engage in various undertakings, and we all hope for the success of our undertakings, but the success of an undertaking depends on whether the overall health environment is suitable as a prerequisite. The so-called suitability of the health environment depends on the extent of the efforts made in public hygiene. Therefore, the quality of public hygiene can predict the success or failure of an undertaking. However, the effectiveness of public hygiene must depend on the efforts of all citizens. Regardless of farmers, workers, merchants, young, old, rich, or poor, everyone should pay close attention to public hygiene. The construction of public hygiene requires the efforts of the masses. Today, there are often people who are selfish and cannot take care of public hygiene. The so-called selfishness is that residents only seek the hygiene of themselves or their families and do not care about others. This kind of harmful behavior is everywhere. For example, some residents often pour sewage and garbage on the streets. They only seek the cleanliness of their own homes, but they do not know that this sewage and garbage is the source of infectious diseases. This kind of behavior is really harmful. I am not a superstitious person, but in fact, due to the prevalence of infectious diseases, one's self is also unavoidable. Therefore, we must publicize this idea to all citizens so that everyone has the common sense of personal hygiene and extends it to the common sense of public hygiene. In other words, everyone can know how to maintain personal hygiene and at the same time pay attention to public hygiene. We deeply know that the cleaning campaign is the basic work for promoting public hygiene, and public hygiene is the prerequisite for the progress of all construction undertakings in the city. If the urban cleaning campaign can be resolved, then public hygiene can also be resolved, creating a very good healthy environment in the city, and everyone can work hard on various construction undertakings. Therefore, the cleaning campaign is very important. I hope that everyone can earnestly persuade the general public to comply. Finally, I will also gather leaders from all walks of life to unite all citizens to create a regular, orderly urban public hygiene. I hope that people will work hard to promote this matter.

Director Zhang's Report (Ye) 110

Mr. Tong's Speech 111

Next, Tong Xingbai, the representative of the Municipal Party Committee, gave a speech, briefly stating that there is actually no distinction between personal and public hygiene in the implementation of hygiene because individuals are a part of the public, and individuals cannot live apart from the public. The relationship between people in society is extremely close. One person is enough to affect the entire society. There is no reason for any individual to be independent in society. If an individual has unsanitary facts, it is enough to hinder the public. Therefore, everyone must be hygienic, and everyone must be healthy, and then the whole society will be blessed. Everyone must not think that the hygiene campaign is a small matter. Its relationship with the country and the nation is not shallow. The low status of our nation and the unhealthy and unsanitary people are the main reasons. In today's world of survival and competition, without healthy citizens, there is no way to talk about excellent culture. Therefore, the hygiene campaign is a national salvation movement. If we think that the hygiene campaign is just to solve the problems of small mosquitoes, garbage, and spitting, then we are only seeing the small and not the big.

Mr. Wang's Speech 112

Finally, Wang Xiaolai of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce gave a speech. Mr. Wang said that the greatest happiness in life is health, and the most important element of health is hygiene. Hygiene must also be accompanied by exercise. Those who are unwilling to exercise must be lazy, and those who are lazy must be unsanitary. This is a connected relationship. I also believe that the hygiene campaign is a major undertaking. Simply cleaning the surface is not enough. We must first clean the hearts of people. Once the heart is filthy, it is useless to clean the surface. Therefore, from today onwards, everyone should first clean the filth of the heart, and second, clean the filth of the body. When everyone's body and mind are cleaned, the public hygiene problem and the health problem will be solved.

Mass Street Sweeping 113

After the speeches, the music played, and the presidium of the conference and all the staff set off to sweep the streets. First, Mayor Wu and the various staff members of the conference took the lead. Each person held a broom, all with handles wrapped in red cloth. After the staff of the conference, the Public Security Bureau military band and

Mayor Wu, Director Li, and Others Personally Sweep Streets (Photo by Xu Tianzhang) 114

police persuasion teams, etc., each held brooms and went to Dalin Road, sweeping from the entrance of the Public Sports Field to the tram tracks on Fangxie Road. Photography reporters from various Chinese and Western newspapers rushed to take pictures of Mayor Wu and participants Pan Gongzhan, Xu Peihuang, Wen Hongen, Li Tingan, Tong Xingbai, etc. After the photos were taken, Mayor Wu and others left in cars, and the police persuasion teams split up and set off into the streets to carry out the street sweeping. The ceremony then came to an end.

Hygiene Lockdown 115

At 2:00 PM, the Municipal Health Bureau issued a hygiene lockdown order. The Municipal Health Bureau posted notices at various public announcement locations, urging citizens throughout the city to abide by the five basic hygiene requirements stipulated in the lockdown order. The New Life Movement persuasion teams, based on the provisions of the lockdown order, verbally persuaded citizens from all walks of life to strictly comply. The Chinese and foreign police agencies also assisted the persuasion teams in enforcing the order. After the hygiene lockdown order was issued, the five items stipulated in the order would be permanently enforced, ensuring that citizens throughout the city would develop these good habits. In order to arouse public attention to the hygiene campaign, the Municipal Health Bureau specially invited Mayor Wu Tiecheng and Tong Xingbai, a standing committee member of the Municipal Party Committee, to broadcast speeches on radio stations at Chinese and Western pharmacies and the Buddhist Sound Broadcasting Station at 4:00 PM (the speeches are published in a special issue).

Vaccination Campaign 116

The vaccination teams organized by the Municipal Health Bureau, the Health Department of the International Settlement, the Health Department of the French Concession, and medical groups are administering vaccinations in various locations starting this afternoon. This vaccination campaign requires all agencies, schools, and factories to be vaccinated by the vaccination teams, and attention will also be paid to vaccinating coolies and poor people along the way. The civil residences sponsored by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau will also have vaccination teams dispatched by the Municipal Health Bureau to force vaccinations. Therefore, the number of people vaccinated has already reached tens of thousands in one day. As for the various rural areas, the Municipal Health Bureau has also ordered various health offices to dispatch vaccination teams to the villages to administer vaccinations.

New Life Movement Persuasion Teams Launch Citywide Campaign Yesterday; Each Team of Three to Five Distributes Covenants, etc., with a Three-Day Deadline; Mixed Persuasion Teams Also Formed 117

The New Life Movement persuasion teams from all walks of life in Shanghai launched a citywide campaign yesterday. After participating in the hygiene campaign at the Public Sports Field at 10:00 AM, they began to persuade people in their respective designated areas.

Starting the Persuasion 118

The persuasion teams from all walks of life, such as Boy Scouts, education sector, police, agricultural sector, industrial sector, business sector, security teams, defense corps, military police, etc., were ordered to participate in the hygiene campaign at the Public Sports Field yesterday morning at 10:00 AM. After the meeting, they began to persuade people in their respective designated areas, braving the rain. Each team consisted of three to five people, with one team leader holding the New Life Movement persuasion flag, distributing leaflets and the New Life Covenant. Mixed persuasion teams were also organized to set off to complex public places.

Scope of Each Team 119

The dates for the citywide launch of the persuasion teams from all walks of life are yesterday, today, and tomorrow. (1) The Boy Scout persuasion team will pay special attention to order in public places and schools, and to the rescue of women, children, the elderly, and the weak. (2) The Church persuasion team will focus especially on schools and students. (3) The Police persuasion team will target ordinary citizens. Any inappropriate attire, bad behavior, spitting, defecating, or children under the age of sixteen smoking cigarettes should be corrected. In addition, the need to vaccinate to avoid smallpox and to be vaccinated against disease should be promoted at any time. For street vendors selling snacks and hotels, taverns, and restaurants, pay attention to cleanliness. (4) The agricultural and industrial persuasion teams will target rural villages, factories, and shops. Hygiene facilities, fire prevention facilities, accommodation, and lifestyles should be guided at any time and place. (5) The Security Team persuasion team should assist the police in persuading citizens in certain situations. (6) The Self-Defense Corps persuasion team will target shops, paying attention to the merchants' gentle attitude, fair transactions, neat attire, and honest language. (7) The Military Police persuasion team will target soldiers, correcting any irregular lifestyle, improper behavior, or rude attitude towards ordinary citizens, as well as failure to pay fares or vehicle fares in public places.

Situation in Western Shanghai 120

Yesterday, all citizens in the Caojiadu area of western Shanghai held a New Life Movement conference. All factories and shops hung flags and lights. At 2:00 PM, the meeting was held in the Caojiadu Self-Defense Corps building. Those who participated in the meeting were quite enthusiastic. The groups included the Citizens' Association Third District Branch, the Self-Defense Corps Second Team, Cao Yi Elementary School, Shixi Elementary School, the Fire Brigade, Yongyi Hall, and other representatives from all walks of life, totaling about 500 people, including Chen Yunquan, Yu Yuqing, District Chief Tan of the Sixth District, Inspector Cheng, Huang Zhihe, Yang Songlin, Xia Botang, and Zheng Liankun. The presidium consisted of Yu Yuqing, Chen Yunquan, and Huang Zhihe. The order was as follows: (1) Play music and start the meeting. (2) All stand up and bow three times. (3) The presidium respectfully reads the will of Dr. Sun Yat-sen. (4) Report the purpose of the meeting and explain the meaning of the New Life Movement. (5) District Chief Tan of the Sixth District elaborates on the implementation of the New Life Movement as a fundamental way to save the country, and explains the four aspects of clothing, food, housing, and transportation in detail, briefly stating that clothing should be clean, neat, simple, and use domestic goods; food should be frugal, on time, hygienic, and cherish leftovers; housing should be swept, orderly, bright, and quiet; and transportation should be dignified, forward and backward, on foot, and in accordance with regulations. Next, Yang Chen elaborates that the New Life Movement must start with the individual. (6) Students from the two schools sing the Party song. (7) Play music. (8) Slogans: The New Life Movement is the national salvation movement; Propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame are the foundation of the nation; Have a modest demeanor; Have a loyal attitude; Have a clean behavior; Be quick to act; Be frugal in life; Obey discipline; Take responsibility; Revitalize the entire nation; Long live the Republic of China. (9) Play music and dismiss the meeting. Afterwards, District Chief Tan personally led the teams with a broom, divided into teams to persuade the people, and swept the roads. In the evening, a lantern parade was held, and the observers on various roads were quite crowded, creating a very lively scene.

Sino-British Bank Annual Meeting Reports Favorable Conditions on Both Railways; Excerpts from the Management Bureau's Report 121

The Management Bureau of the Jinpu Railway and the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway issued a statement that the 36th Annual General Meeting of Shareholders of the Sino-British Bank was held at the company's office at 3 Lombard Street in London. Mr. Pinatt presided over the meeting, and Mr. Pinatt reported in detail on the recent conditions of China's state-owned railways. Excerpts related to both railways are as follows:

Jinpu Railway 122

The damage suffered by the railway in 1932 has been repaired, and work has returned to normal. The financial situation is also stable. The total income for this year (referring to 1922) is 13.5 million yuan, an increase of approximately 4 million yuan compared to the previous year. Due to the establishment of the ferry between Xiaguan and Pukou and the addition of vehicles to develop combined transport operations, the railway had to allocate a portion of its income to capital expenditure, which has limited its debt repayment capacity to some extent. The proposal to relocate the Shanghai Main Station is still pending. The railway's main office was bombed by aircraft in 1932. The original site has now been rebuilt and allocated to the Transportation Department for office use. The funds borrowed from the company in 1929 to purchase vehicles are now being used to develop business and cope with competition. The funds allocated by the railway to the company for debt repayment have been received on time each month. Since the completion of the Yangtze River railway ferry linking the Tianjin-Pukou line, the progress in income has been extremely significant, and the future prospects are bright. As for expenditures, there is still room for economy in the future. The Chinese and British staff of the railway get along very well, and there is no animosity between them. Their hard work is admirable and deserves to be commended. The railway's finances have gradually improved through gradual reforms. Even the originally overdue interest coupons from 1932 were paid off at the end of last year. The dividends due to the holder of the 1929 net profit coupons were paid in October. Although there are still some outstanding payments, unless there is an unforeseen event that the Chinese government has never been willing to succumb to, there will be no obstacles to the future development of the railway, and the date of its recovery can be counted on fingers.

Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway 123

During the year, the total income of the railway has exceeded 6 million yuan, almost equivalent to the previous year's figures. The ability to repay debt is improving day by day. Since June 1922, the amount of special reserve funds on the account has been increased from 10% to 20% of the total income. In addition, a certain amount has been withdrawn from the surplus income of the Jinpu Railway as a reserve for debt repayment. The amount due for withdrawal in June last year, which has not been paid, will now be prepared on schedule so that the Sino-British bonds will be fully repaid by the end of the year. The Chinese government is now working hard to complete the unfinished sections of the line and to build the Qiantang River Bridge in Hangzhou. If both of these come to fruition, then the sharp increase in the railway's income in the future is a matter of course.

Wu Tiecheng Talks: Chiang Kai-shek to Go to Jiangxi to Supervise the Suppression; Whether to Go to Hangzhou to Return to His Ancestral Home is Undecided 124

According to the Central News Agency, after Chairman Chiang Kai-shek returned to Nanjing from Jiangxi, it was rumored that Chiang would go to Hangzhou to return to his ancestral home within days. However, according to Mayor Wu Tiecheng yesterday, it has not yet been decided whether Chiang will return to Fenghua. However, it is known that Chiang will not stay in Nanjing for long and will have to go to Jiangxi to supervise the suppression of the remaining bandits.

Northeast Association Seeks Conclusion 125

The Northeast Association's solicitation of members ended the day before yesterday. The total number of members is about 300, of which the number of friends in Peiping is the largest, accounting for one-third, and the rest are mostly people from Beijing, Shanghai, and other places. In addition, the Association's reelection of the second session of directors will be held at the beginning of next month, after the Association's acting secretary, Qi Shiying, comes to Shanghai, and then the reelection will begin using communication methods.

Page 10

Pirates Hijack New Shuntian Steamer; Shanghai News: One Crew Member Shot; Sixteen People Abducted; Valuables Looted; Cargo Holds and Machinery Untouched 126

The New Shuntian, a steamship of the Southern Taikoo Line that had been built at the Hong Kong shipyard and sent to Shanghai to replace the old Shunda steamer on the North China route, set sail on its maiden voyage from Shanghai on June 2. Then, on the 17th, on its second voyage from Shanghai to Tianjin, when it was sailing from Tanggu to Zhifu at about 10:30 p.m., it was hijacked by pirates. The terrifying case involved the shooting of a crew member and the abduction of a large number of Chinese and foreign passengers and crew members, totaling twenty-six. The details are as follows:

Pirates Planned for a Long Time 127

When the British firm Ewo Yanghsing's Yisheng steamer was robbed, the bandits told the people on board that they had originally intended to rob a Taikoo's northbound steamer, but because there were too many people on board and the defenses were stricter, they did not dare to do so, so they changed to rob the Yisheng steamer. This matter was reported in the newspaper. After the six people on board the Yisheng steamer were kidnapped, months have passed, and they have not yet been rescued. Now, the Taikoo's New Shuntian steamer has been hijacked again. The pirates have been planning the robbery for a long time, not just for a day or two.

Bandits Disembarked from Tianjin 128

The New Shuntian steamer has a very good passenger seat layout, so it has more passengers than other steamers. This time, when it sailed south from Tianjin, the ship carried more than 300 first-, second-, and third-class passengers. About 30 pirates disguised themselves as passengers in Tianjin and boarded the ship. After boarding the ship, they scattered in the various cabin levels. When the steamer sailed from Tanggu at 10:30 p.m., when the passengers were sound asleep, the ship had already sailed near the mouth of the Yellow River. The pirates who had mixed in the ship then sneaked up to the deck from the various cabins. They were very familiar with the ship's route, and it seemed that they had already seen it clearly in advance. As soon as the pirates appeared, several pirates occupied the ship's radio room. The pirates drew their guns and forced the radio operator to go to the smoking room and detain him there. Then, they divided up and began to rob.

All Crew Members Imprisoned 129

When the radio operator was detained, the ship's captain, Mr. Christie, suddenly heard urgent footsteps and noisy voices on the ship. He rushed out of the captain's room to investigate. However, as soon as Mr. Christie reached the door, he was captured by three pirates who had been lying in wait outside. They used guns to stop his movements and escorted him to the smoking room and detained him there. At that time, the third officer, Mr. Ross, who was on duty, was driving the ship. The pirates forced him to leave the ship. Ross refused and resisted the pirates. He was shot and wounded by the pirates. Two other crew members and two engine crew members were also forced to be detained in the smoking room, guarded by several pirates.

Pirates Control the Ship 130

After the crew members were detained, the entire ship was under the control of the pirates. When the ship was sailing, the management of the engine was handed over to a pirate to drive. The pirate had considerable maritime experience. The direction of the ship had gradually changed and was heading towards the mouth of the Yellow River. The pirates then went in batches to the passengers in each cabin and began to rob them. The looted items were temporarily placed in the smoking room. The New Shuntian steamer ran aground at the mouth of the Yellow River from 4:00 a.m. on the 18th until it floated out after the robbery, lasting a total of twelve hours.

Passengers Looted 131

During the search, almost all passengers in the cabins of all levels were spared. All cash, jewelry, clothing, and other items were looted. The bandits searched the ship several times, lasting twelve hours. Even the passengers' luggage, baskets, and bags were opened and searched. Among the passengers, there were ten foreign men and women. The British Consul in Qingdao, Mr. Lyle, and his wife were also on board. The bandits selected clothes that fit their bodies from the looted clothes and changed into them in the ship, and threw the original worn clothes into the cabins.

Abduction of Passengers Before Departure 132

At 2:00 p.m. on the 18th, the bandits packed the looted silver and jewelry and first arranged for five civilian boats to stop on the ship's side. When the pirates were about to leave, they abducted twenty-one passengers from the first- and second-class cabins, and wanted to kidnap four foreign passengers and two crew members. As a result, they abducted five people, including the Westerners Nico Pfeiffer, Ross, Third Officer Wasson, Second Officer Breit, and the Japanese Yamamoto. The twenty-six Chinese and foreign people were then escorted onto the civilian boats and fled.

Electric Shanghai Reports Robbery 133

After the bandits left, the captain, Mr. Christie, and the Chinese comprador, Sun Rangsan, sent a radio message to Shanghai, briefly stating that the New Shuntian steamer had been robbed, the Chinese crew members were safe, and asked to inform their families. Third Officer Ross was shot and injured and was in critical condition. Second Officer Si and three Western passengers and twenty-one Chinese passengers were kidnapped. After the crew members on board escaped, they first repaired the radio. The captain also sent a distress call. The stranded ship floated up at high tide and corrected its course to head towards Yantai. All the weapons on board had been looted by the bandits, but the cargo holds had not been opened and the machinery had not been damaged, so it could still sail.

Warships Rushed to Escort 134

The British destroyer HMS Witch, stationed in Weihaiwei, and the American destroyer stationed in Yantai rushed to the mouth of the Yellow River after receiving a telegram from the New Shuntian. The New Shuntian happened to meet them on the way and was escorted to Zhifu. On the morning of the 19th,

the ship finally arrived in Yantai under the protection of a British warship. After the ship stopped, the seriously injured Third Officer Ross was first sent to the American Hospital for emergency treatment. After loading passengers in Yantai, the ship set sail for Qingdao at 9:00 a.m.

Ships Expected in Shanghai This Afternoon 135

The Xinshun Tian Steamer is currently en route, and the journey from Yantai to Qingdao takes approximately eighteen hours. After a brief stop in Qingdao, it will continue to Shanghai, with an additional twenty-five hours of travel time. Therefore, it is estimated that the Xinshun Tian Steamer will arrive at the port this afternoon. Upon arrival in Shanghai, the ship will dock at Pier No. 3 in the French Concession along the Xinkai River. Details regarding the hijacking and the extent of the losses will be available once the ship arrives in Shanghai.

Chinese and Foreign Troops Sent to Pursue and Suppress 136

Following the incident, warships from the British and American navies stationed in Yantai and Weihaiwei have been dispatched to patrol the ports of Tanggu, Yantai, and the Bohai Sea to pursue and apprehend the pirates. Han Fuqu, the Chairman of Shandong Province, also received a telegram from the Yantai local authorities and dispatched land and naval forces to cooperate with the British and American warships in searching the coastal areas.

Status of Post-Incident Measures 137

The Taikoo Dockyard Company was shocked by the news. Now they are waiting for the ship to arrive in Shanghai and have decided to add anti-theft iron netting to the ship and increase the escort team to ensure maritime safety. Since yesterday, they have ordered all departing ships to take strict precautions. Yesterday, the Suzhou steamer, which departed from Shanghai for Qingdao, stopped carrying passengers. Furthermore, when the Xin Shengjing steamer departed for Beiyang, the company specially dispatched three inspectors to board the ship and search the passengers. The Jianghai Customs also dispatched a small vessel to accompany the Shengjing, inspecting passengers in all classes of cabins along the way until it returned to Wusong. The British Navy even sent a warship to accompany the ship for protection. According to the Da Mei Evening News, news was received in Shanghai today (the 19th) that the British warship [name missing] is preparing to leave Weihaiwei immediately, carrying multiple aircraft. If the Chinese authorities permit British aircraft to operate within Chinese territory, the aircraft will be used to scout for the pirates who hijacked the Shuntian steamer in order to rescue those who were kidnapped.

Overseas Chinese in Japan Expelled and Escorted Back Home; Chen Chongshan and 15 Others Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday; Property Confiscated; Plight Wretched; Going to Beijing Today to Report Petition and Negotiate 138

According to the Dagong News Agency, more than 20 overseas Chinese from Wenzhou and other places in China were living in Yonezawa City, Yamagata Prefecture, Japan, which is an ordinary city. They established a total of 13 restaurants, and for eight years, they had lived in relative harmony. However, since the September 18th Incident, the local authorities in that area had been making things difficult for the overseas Chinese in every way, and they had been subjected to insults and abuses, which they could only endure in silence. In June of this year, Yoshimura, the police chief of the Yonezawa City Police Station, suddenly dispatched numerous police officers, using the excuse that they needed to renew their business licenses, otherwise they would be banned. However, the overseas Chinese had been doing business for many years, and according to the usual practice, they had renewed their licenses in April of each year as required, and this year they had also been renewed, so why were there any additional complications? The police station refused to listen to explanations and immediately dispatched police to arrest and detain all the overseas Chinese. Wang Hongnian, the Chinese Consul in Yokohama, made representations to Sato, the Director of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, but to no avail. They were detained for two nights. On the 10th of this month, more than ten maritime police officers were dispatched to escort all the overseas Chinese to Osaka, where they stayed overnight. On the 12th, the overseas Chinese were escorted to Yokohama, boarded the Japanese cargo ship Tsukuba Maru, and returned to their home country. All their property was confiscated. The overseas Chinese arrived in Shanghai at 4 p.m. the day before yesterday, and the ship docked at the Huishan Pier in Hongkou, where their plight was quite wretched.

Names of the Distressed Overseas Chinese 139

After arriving in Shanghai, the distressed overseas Chinese were unfamiliar with the local conditions and had nowhere to turn. Fortunately, a fellow Wenzhou native, Mr. Zhu, ran a hotel in Nanshi and offered to take care of them. A reporter from the Dagong News Agency went to investigate and found the names of the overseas Chinese to be: Hu Zhichao, Chen Xitie, Chen Chongshan, Wu Defa, Zheng Xipeng, Ye Shengyi, Zhu Yisheng, Dong Duanjun, Zhu Guimiao, Zhu Tongsheng, Wei Lianchang, Zhu Tonglian, Xu Tingfang, Wu Zhengxiang, and Hu Zhaoqing, 16 people in total.

Petition for Relief 140

The distressed overseas Chinese lacked travel expenses to return to their hometowns and felt it was difficult to stay in Shanghai. Furthermore, they planned to go to Beijing to report to the central government and request negotiations. Therefore, at 10 a.m. yesterday, they sent representatives Hu Zhichao, Chen Chongxi, and five others to the Fenglinqiao Municipal Party Headquarters to petition for relief. Zhang Zixiao, the Director of the General Affairs Section of the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Yu Yaoqiu, a clerk from the Investigation Section, received them, inquired about the details of their expulsion, and the overseas Chinese presented various supporting documents. Mr. Zhang and others expressed that they would find a way to provide relief.

Heading to Beijing Today 141

The Municipal Party Headquarters further investigated and found that all 16 of the distressed overseas Chinese were members of the Kuomintang. The main reason for their expulsion was their participation in patriotic movements in Japan, which aroused the Japanese authorities' jealousy. Therefore, they dispatched Yu Yaoqiu, a clerk from the Investigation Section, to contact the Red Cross Society, which issued them ship tickets. They are scheduled to take a boat to Beijing this afternoon to report the details of their expulsion to the Central Party Headquarters and request that the matter be referred to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for serious negotiations in order to safeguard the safety of overseas Chinese.

Confiscated Property 142

The distressed overseas Chinese Chen Chongshan, according to the Dagong News Agency reporter, had been doing business in Japan for many years and had accumulated some savings. All the property that was confiscated by the police station during this expulsion and the amounts of the losses are as follows: The Chunghua Restaurant in Yakushiro-cho lost 1,000 yuan; the Shanghai Xuan Restaurant in Tatsumachi lost 1,500 yuan; the Baolai Xuan Restaurant in Doumachi lost 1,100 yuan; the Nanjing [Restaurant] in Yoshicho lost 1,000 yuan; the Baoliang Xuan Restaurant in Kantomachi lost 800 yuan; the [Restaurant] in Tatsumachi lost 1,100 yuan; the Zhejiang Xuan Restaurant in Omachi lost 900 yuan; the Chunghua Xuan Restaurant in Menkyo-cho lost 1,500 yuan; the New Chunghua Xuan Restaurant in Nagamachi lost 600 yuan; the Kairai Xuan Restaurant in Onogawa Onsen lost 500 yuan; the Fanyi Xuan Restaurant in Komatsucho lost 1,300 yuan; the Chunghua Xuan Restaurant in Miyauchicho lost 500 yuan; and the Chunghua Xuan Restaurant in Yunoseng-mura lost 300 yuan, totaling approximately 10,000 to 20,000 yuan.

A Letter to Compatriots 143

In order to make our compatriots aware of the recent treatment of overseas Chinese by Japan, the distressed overseas Chinese drafted a detailed report to the compatriots across the country, which reads as follows: To all newspaper offices, comrades, and compatriots across the country: We, the overseas Chinese residing in Japan, have been subjected to oppression by the Japanese people for a long time. Numerous people have returned to China one after another, but the people of our country have been indifferent to this, which is a great sigh. Our government has not made efforts to protect us, and our compatriots have not given us great assistance, so that countless weak overseas Chinese have been humiliated by the Japanese people and have been crying overseas. Recently, sixteen overseas Chinese residing in Yonezawa City, Yamagata Prefecture, Japan, were arrested and imprisoned by the Japanese police authorities, their property was confiscated, and they were ordered to return to their home country. On the 10th of this month, they were humiliated and returned on the Tsukuba Maru from Yokohama and arrived in Shanghai on the 18th. We, the overseas Chinese, have been doing business in Yonezawa City for more than eight years, and we have all been diligent, thrifty, cautious, and self-reliant, so we have accumulated some savings to this day. However, since the September 18th Incident, the city police station has often unreasonably oppressed and humiliated us, which is truly unacceptable. We believe that our motherland is in a time of trouble, and the national crisis is serious. We are deeply moved by the fate of the people of the secondary colonial countries who endure humiliation and hardship. We are deeply aware of the responsibility of uniting overseas Chinese to save the country from danger. Otherwise, we will be slaughtered by others forever. Temporary humiliation can only be endured. Although there have been incidents in which the Japanese police stopped business operations from time to time, after negotiations, they were still able to operate as usual. Unexpectedly, on the 2nd of last month, the city police station repeated its old tricks and went even further, arresting and imprisoning all the overseas Chinese in Yonezawa City without any reason, and ordering us, the overseas Chinese, to forcibly pay 35 yen each before the 15th as travel expenses to return to our home country. When asked why they were escorting all the overseas Chinese in Yonezawa City back to their home country, they replied that restaurants should have licenses, and since [you] do not have licenses, you should be banned. We have investigated that all the overseas Chinese in Yonezawa City have the licenses, and they have been doing business there for more than eight years. Every April, they renew them according to the rules. However, this year, they have already submitted the licenses from last year and asked them to renew them, but the authorities not only did not issue them, but said that since there are no licenses, they should be banned. It is extremely lawless. Furthermore, after the overseas Chinese were arrested and imprisoned in the police station, all their property was confiscated. Old debts were not allowed to be recovered, and new savings were all in vain. Alas, the hard work of the overseas Chinese, the blood and sweat of several years, were all gone in one morning. There was no response to heaven, and there was no way to ask for help. Although we begged the Consul General in Yokohama to ask our country's ambassador to Japan to negotiate with the Japanese government with all our strength, it was to no avail. Therefore, on the 10th of this month, we were ordered by the police to take the Japanese cargo ship Tsukuba Maru from Yokohama back to our home country and arrived in Shanghai on the 18th. Furthermore, five of the overseas Chinese had been living in Japan for a long time, married Japanese women, and had children. The five Japanese women, due to the love between husband and wife, returned to their home country with them, hoping to grow old together. However, when the ship arrived in Kobe, they were also detained by the maritime police and were not allowed to return with the overseas Chinese. Alas, young children have become fatherless, and young women have become wifeless. Anyone with a little heart would feel sad when they hear about it. Marriage freedom is permitted by Japanese law, but the Japanese police persecute us regardless of right and wrong. Their inhumanity is unimaginable. We deeply hope that compatriots across the country will rise up and rescue us. It is not too late to mend the fold after the sheep is lost. Otherwise, the remaining overseas Chinese in Japan will be trampled on by this poisonous tooth and iron hoof one after another. This is a joint statement from the overseas Chinese in Yonezawa City, Japan.

Construction Committee Plans to Build the Beijing-Zhao'an Railway, Approximately 1,200 Kilometers Long, Running Through Four Provinces; Construction Can Begin Soon 144

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, in order to complete the southeastern transportation network, the Construction Committee, in addition to having the Jiangnan Railway Company construct the Wuhu-Zhejiang Railway to connect with the Eastern Great Port, has recently planned to construct the Beijing-Zhao'an Railway, which will start from Nanjing and go directly to Zhao'an at the southern end of Fujian, with a total length of approximately 1,200 kilometers. The project is now being carried out by Hong Kun, the chief engineer of the Wuhu-Zhejiang Railway, and the project is planned to be divided into five sections: (1) The Beijing-Wuhu Section, that is, from Nanjing to Wuhu in Anhui; (2) The Wuhu-Sunjiafu Section, that is, from Wuhu to Sunjiafu, which can borrow a section of the Wuhu-Zhejiang Railway and does not need to be built separately; (3) The Sunjiafu-Jiangshan Section, that is, from Sunjiafu to Jiangshan in Zhejiang Province; (4) The Jiangshan-Yanping Section, that is, from Jiangshan to Yanping in Fujian Province; (5) The Yanping-Zhao'an Section, that is, from Yanping to Zhao'an in southern Fujian. Except for the Wuhu-Sunjiafu Section, the remaining four sections of the project will be completed in four phases. It is expected that the first phase of the Beijing-Wuhu Section will begin construction soon. The total cost is 30 million yuan. If the railway is completed, the railways of Jiangsu, Anhui, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Fujian, and Guangdong provinces can be directly connected.

Eurasia Aviation Company's Lanzhou-Ningxia Route Opened Yesterday 145

In order to develop transportation in the northwest, the Eurasia Aviation Company has opened the Lanzhou-Ningxia route and officially started operating from Shanghai at 8 a.m. yesterday. The route is only 400 kilometers long and can be reached in two hours. It is one of the branch lines of the Eurasia route. It is scheduled to take off from Shanghai every Tuesday at 8 a.m., arrive in Xi'an on the same day, stay overnight, arrive in Lanzhou at 11 a.m. the next day, and fly to Ningxia in the afternoon. At 4:30 p.m., it can fly back to Lanzhou, stay overnight, and then return to Shanghai along the original route the next day. Although the distance between Lanzhou and Ningxia is not far, transportation is inconvenient and travel is difficult. Therefore, after the opening of the route, transportation between the two places has been greatly facilitated. (Central News Agency)

Wang Yansong Resigns from the Supervisory Committee of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce 148

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, Wang Yansong, the newly elected member of the Supervisory Committee of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, was originally a Standing Committee member of the Chamber of Commerce for four years. At the end of the current term, he was not allowed to be re-elected in accordance with the regulations. However, Wang was extremely enthusiastic and responsible in handling the affairs of the Chamber of Commerce and safeguarding commerce during his tenure. During the turbulent times, he experienced many difficulties. During the January 28th Incident, Shanghai was the first to bear the brunt, and he experienced panic and shock. He was able to calmly deal with the situation and avoid difficulties, so he was deeply trusted by representatives of all industries. In this re-election, he was still elected as a member of the Supervisory Committee by a majority. However, Wang wanted to rest and recuperate after serving for a long time, so he wrote to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday to request his resignation. The original letter is recorded as follows: "To the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce: I, Yansong, have completed my current term, and I hope to have a temporary rest with the protection of laws and regulations. Unexpectedly, the election results still have me as a member of the Supervisory Committee. Public opinion is where it is, and it is difficult to let down [the public]. My private feelings are really regrettable. Thinking that I have worked hard in commercial transportation for many years, from being entrusted by the central government to unify the merchant organizations, to legally establishing the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, I have been elected as a Standing Committee member for six years. In the past, it was always difficult for the group meetings to meet the legal quorum, and those who were scattered and undisciplined criticized it. I, Yansong, uphold the principle, engage in unity, work hard, and do not avoid resentment. Fortunately, following the members, I can avoid mistakes. In terms of merchant organizations, they are now slightly better than in the past. In addition, I have strived to seek welfare and reduce pain as much as possible. On the Jing [Beijing] Road, I have been busy with official documents and appeals. My humble heart is only to ensure that the business community does its best and contributes its meager efforts to fulfill its responsibilities to the utmost. In recent years, I have felt tired and tired. I hope to take a small break when I resign. Fortunately, the newly elected gentlemen are all outstanding talents, and the re-elected members are familiar with the work. The Chamber of Commerce will prosper and develop in the future. I, Yansong, as a leisurely person, am fortunate to see the vigorous image. All the duties of the Supervisory Committee are hereby solemnly declared, and I will no longer be re-elected. The intention is sincere, and the matter is not hypocritical. Please approve the resignation and [follow] the regulations to replace me. I am deeply honored."

Shanghai-Tongguan Joint Transportation of Goods by Beijing-Shanghai, Tianjin-Pukou, and Longhai Railways Has Been Implemented; Designated Downstream Train No. 403 and Upstream Train No. 404; When the Goods Are Not Enough for One Train, They Can Be Attached to the Shanghai-Beiping Freight Train 149

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, since the Shanghai-Beiping joint transportation of freight trains was implemented, the Beijing-Shanghai, Tianjin-Pukou, and Longhai Railway Bureaus have opened joint transportation of freight trains since last month. The joint transportation of goods from various stations on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway to various stations on the Longhai Railway, or from various stations on the Longhai Railway to various stations on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, are all attached to the downstream train No. 401 Ping-Hu freight train and the upstream train No. 402 Hu-Ping freight train. Initially, it only reached Zhengzhou Station on the Longhai Railway, but now it has been extended to Tongguan Station. Downstream train No. 403 and upstream train No. 404 are designated as Shanghai-Tongguan joint transportation trains. If the joint transportation goods carried are not enough for one train, they can be attached to the Shanghai-Beiping freight train. For example, the freight train from Shanghai to Tongguan is attached to the No. 402 Hu-Ping freight train and unloaded at Xuzhou Station on the Tianjin-Pukou Railway, and then attached to the Longhai Railway freight train to open to Tongguan. The freight train from Tongguan to Shanghai is attached to the No. 401 Ping-Hu freight train and transported to Shanghai after arriving at Xuzhou Station on the Tianjin-Pukou Railway. Shanghai and Tongguan depart once a day.

Jianghai Customs Permits Inland Water Vessels to Carry Goods According to Past Practice; After Requesting the Inland Water Vessel Association, the Customs Commissioner Replied and Approved Accommodations 150

The Municipal Inland Water Vessel Industry Association previously reported that the vessels carried goods, and they used to declare to the Jianghai Customs in advance. For the number of items, they usually only declared a certain number of general merchandise. The method has been followed for a long time. Recently, the Jianghai Customs suddenly changed the past practice and not only required the item names to be listed in detail on the total manifest, but also required the number of items to be reported temporarily before customs clearance was allowed. The association believed that although the vessels carried goods, most of them were temporarily brought by passengers. If they were handled in accordance with the regulations, not only would it be impossible in fact, but also it would not be possible in terms of customs clearance time, which would affect the operations of shipping companies. Therefore, the association sent a letter to the Jianghai Customs Commissioner and sent personnel to explain the difficulties in person, requesting that the past practice be followed. After that, the association received a reply from Customs Commissioner Borlet, which stated, "The case has been approved in accordance with letter No. 77, which stated that according to the Minnan-Shanghai and other shipping companies, the customs clearance methods for vessels carrying goods have been followed for a long time, and the Jianghai Customs has suddenly changed the past practice, which is inconvenient in fact. It is requested that the past practice be followed. After checking, it is known that these shipping companies only travel to and from inland rivers and do not sail out of Wusong, so it can be approved that only the general situation of the goods needs to be declared on the manifest, and no detailed [registration] is required. However, the inspection procedures stipulated by the customs must be strictly followed. Accordingly, I hope that you will check and inform the shipping companies separately, and provide convenience for them." It is heard that the association has recorded the letter and notified all its member companies to check and handle it.

Communist Party Member Li Junshan's Declaration of Surrender 153

According to the Central News Agency, Li Junshan (Ding Junshan) joined the CY Shanghai West Street Branch after the January 28th Incident in December of the 21st year because he felt that the national affairs were in danger at that time. He temporarily felt the words of his friend Zhou Daokuan, saying that the Communist Party's leadership was based on [illegible]. In the 22nd year, the Jiangsu CY Provincial Committee established a distribution department, and he was transferred to be a cadre of the department. In April, he was transferred to be the head of the distribution department. In May, he contracted enteritis and was hospitalized for surgery. The process was not good, and he almost died in the hospital. In July, the disease was cured, and he resumed his relationship and continued his original work. In November, he lost contact for a long time due to the destruction of the organization. It was not until March of the 23rd year that he resumed work, and it was not until now that he realized and surrendered, and issued a declaration saying, "During my work in the Communist Party, I have become disillusioned with the Communist Party, and I have always thought of breaking away, but I am still bound by moral responsibility and still have no courage. Recently, I was guided and persuaded by my predecessors and comrades of the Kuomintang, and I suddenly realized that my political journey had gone astray. The suffering I have endured in my work is due to the fact that the Communist Party's political theory is wrong and the Communist Party's organization's class struggle. At this critical juncture of China's crisis, it is not only not needed by workers and peasants, and it cannot improve the lives of workers and peasants, but it also creates division and destruction of national unity and the crime of concluding an anti-imperialist united front. Therefore, China not only at present, but also in the future, only requires a national united front to fight against domestic and foreign feudal and imperialist forces, and does not need class struggle. Therefore, I resolutely abandon my past position and work hard under the principle of democracy in the interest of the nation, and stand on the forefront of anti-communism. I hope that people who are wandering in the Communist Party will quickly realize [their mistakes]."

Huge Sum Robbed from E Yuen Dog Racing Track; Robbers Mostly from Bourgeois Class; One Owns a Hardware Store, One a Major Shareholder in a Distilling Company; Due to Seriousness of Case, Court Refuses Bail 156

At the E Yuen Dog Racing Track on Avenue Albert in the French Concession, on the 9th of this month, at approximately 4 PM, employees Gao Yushu, Mr. Fan, and Mr. Hong, each carrying $6,000 in cash, hired a car to deliver the funds to accountant Xue Mai Luo's office at 9 Avenue Edward VII for accounting purposes. Upon arriving at the destination, Gao and others alighted from the car. Just as they entered the clerical office of Xue Mai Luo's accounting firm, four robbers, well-dressed and with fierce expressions, resembling upper-class individuals, suddenly appeared. Each pulled out a pistol and warned them not to make a sound. They robbed Gao and Fan of $12,000 in cash ($6,000 each), then fled the scene in a rush. The incident was reported to the French police for investigation. Around 6 PM on the 15th, the victim, Gao Yushu, while passing by the Guangxi Road branch of the Good Friends Automobile Company in the Public Concession, spotted one of the robbers entering the car dealership to hire a car. Gao immediately reported this to the French police. Inspector Jin Jiulin and detective Zhang Ziying and others tracked the car to a brothel, where they apprehended the robber, identified as Zhang Zuming, 28 years old, from Ningbo. Zhang confessed that he owned the Ruichangshun Hardware Store at 101 Broadway Road and identified two accomplices: Zhuang Jimeng, 21 years old, from Ningbo, a minor shareholder in the Zhuang Yuan Distilling Company at 42 Avenue Westward, currently serving as a special patrolman in the Public Concession police force (Note: Zhuang Yuan has been in business for decades and is famous far and wide, especially for its Dou Shao wine); and Wang Lianyou, 30 years old, from Ningbo, a hardware broker residing at 931 Xiang Yu Xiang Yu Lane, Avenue du Roi Albert. The detectives then arrested Zhuang and Wang, seizing two pistols, and brought them back to the police station. All three defendants were men of status and wealth. Yesterday afternoon, they were escorted to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court, where Judge Li Changnian presided over the hearing. The police lawyer, Fei Xizhen, stated that the defendants were arrested for robbery and that the police needed more time to investigate and requested that the defendants be detained for two more weeks to clarify the details of the case before filing charges. Detective Zhang Ziying then reported the circumstances of the arrest. Gao Yushu, 29 years old, from Tianjin, and one of the victims, testified that he worked for Xue Mai Luo’s accounting firm. During the robbery, the first and third defendants entered first, followed by the second defendant and another suspect who is still at large. He recognized the faces of the first defendant and others, and they were the ones who took the cash from him. The plaintiff's lawyer, Yan Luqing, made a statement, requesting to file a private suit to recover the stolen money. The defendants each retained a lawyer. After a brief interrogation, the court adjourned the hearing until the 23rd. The defendants were remanded in custody. The defendants' lawyers requested bail, but the court rejected the request due to the seriousness of the case. It should be noted that the E Yuen Dog Racing Track was robbed of $6,000 on May 13th of last year while sending employees to deliver funds to 9 Avenue Edward VII. One robber was caught and brought to court. This is the second robbery.

The U.S. Silver Purchase Act has been officially passed. Recently, several shipments of silver have been exported from Shanghai to various countries in the United States and England. Yesterday, another large shipment of silver dollars was loaded for the United States. Details are as follows:

Two Million to the U.S. 158

After the passage of the U.S. Silver Purchase Act, there is an urgent need to purchase silver to replenish reserves. Foreign banks in Shanghai have recently purchased a large amount of silver from the city and other regions, much of which is in the form of silver dollars, the national currency in circulation, totaling over two million dollars. Twenty Million to England 159

Quiet Abode Temple Road; Inside Story of Roulette Gambling Den with Many Layers; One Shareholder Takes Gambling Equipment to Tianjin, Fails to Expand; Shanghai Defendants Sentenced Separately; Fugitives Being Hunted by Police 160

The roulette gambling den at 204 Jingan Temple Road on Seymour Road was raided by the Jingan Temple police on the night of the 9th of this month, as reported in the previous newspaper. It is now known that the organization of the gambling den was very tight, with a large internal scale. The managers were ostensibly Frenchmen named Sharaineau and Marcel, but in reality, many more Chinese participated, such as Wang Wenan, former manager of the Great China Dance Hall and current shareholder of a certain company, as well as Zhou Sifu, Li Zigang, and others, all of whom were shareholders in the gambling den. Since its establishment, the gambling den has been extremely popular every night, with winnings reaching several million dollars. The amount of losses can often be seen. However, the shareholders were still not satisfied and wanted to expand to Tianjin. Several days before the raid, a certain shareholder was specially dispatched to take the roulette gambling equipment by ship to Tianjin. Unexpectedly, the plan was not kept secret. When the ship arrived in Tianjin, customs officers boarded the ship for inspection and confiscated the gambling equipment. The person carrying the equipment, seeing the failure of the mission and fearing the recriminations from other shareholders in the future, immediately wrote a letter to Wang Wenan. Wang and others were at a loss when the gambling den in Shanghai was also raided, and many employees and gamblers were arrested. Therefore, the escaped shareholders had to retreat and disappear. Among those arrested, besides Sharaineau and two other Frenchmen and five gamblers from Wuxi and three Americans, who were handed over to their respective consulates for investigation, Wang Yaosheng, currently an accountant at the Great Shanghai Dance Hall, as well as Long A’er, Jin A’sheng, and the Russian Su Haier Majialuotian, were handed over to the First Special District Court. The police lawyer, Zhang Shizhu, charged them with gambling and skimming profits and presented a letter found on Wang Yaosheng from Ding Songquan in Tianjin to Wang Wenan, reporting the seizure of the gambling equipment by Tianjin Customs. After Judge Huang interrogated the defendants, he ordered them to post bail of $5,000 each pending further investigation. Yesterday, Judge Huang continued the hearing and rendered a verdict. Wang Yaosheng and Long A’er were sentenced to one month in prison and fined $500 each. Majialuofuf was fined $500. During the appeal period, Wang and Long each had to post $5,000 bail. A’sheng was found not guilty. When the police conducted the investigation, it was difficult to ascertain the details of the gambling den due to its tight organization. Therefore, the subsequent raid required a lot of effort. However, Wang Wenan and others managed to escape and remain at large. In order to completely eliminate the harm caused by roulette gambling dens, the police authorities are strictly pursuing the fugitives.

Kerosene Prices Rise Again; Increase of Fifty Cents per Ten Gallons; Gasoline Prices Also to Rise Next Month 165

Since Russian oil has been actively imported and dumped in China, British and American oil companies have once competed fiercely by drastically lowering prices in order to maintain their market share in China. Later, the three parties, feeling that the losses were too great, formed an agreement and began to raise prices and stop competing. Recently, prices have risen again. Details are as follows:

Kerosene Prices Rise Again 166

The four major oil companies in this city, Texaco, Mobil, Oil Fields, and Asiatic Petroleum, in order to recover the losses from the price war in the past two years, formed an agreement to raise prices uniformly. Texaco suddenly broke the agreement in May and lowered prices again, but the other three companies remained united and maintained the original price of $7.20 per gallon while negotiating with Texaco. It is now known that Texaco has restored the original price. At the same time, starting yesterday, all four companies uniformly raised the price to $7.70 per ten gallons. It is said that they plan to continue to raise prices in the future.

Asiatic Seeks to Manipulate the Market 167

The kerosene and gasoline sold by the British Asiatic Petroleum Company are originally products of the Anglo-Persian Oil Company. The quality of the oil is excellent. In order to monopolize the oil market in East Asia, it is making every effort to expand its assets and control the market. It believes that unless there are other oil company organizations in East Asia besides the original four major oil companies, it will overcome all difficulties and try to suppress and eliminate them.

Gasoline Prices Also to Rise 168

As for gasoline prices, the four major oil companies originally planned to raise prices at the same time as kerosene, but because the distribution method has not yet been agreed upon, they are temporarily maintaining the original selling price of $8.10 per ten gallons. It is heard that the major oil companies in this city are planning everything and plan to raise prices next month.

Establishment of Shanghai County Women's Association 169

On June 17th, the Shanghai Women's Association held an inaugural meeting at the Beiqiao County Party Headquarters. More than 40 members attended. The meeting began at 9 AM with formal ceremonies. Lu Xifang was the chairman and Wu Zhiqin was the recorder. After the chairman reported on the preparations, representatives from the county party, Zhang Jingye, the county government, Wang Xuepeng, the county education bureau, Zheng Guoqi, and the First District, Wang Benda, gave speeches. The meeting then passed the constitution and discussed proposals. Important proposals included: (1) Suggesting that the county education bureau establish adult schools for women; (2) Suggesting that the county education bureau instruct local social education institutions to establish nurseries; (3) Planning to promote women's occupations to improve their livelihoods; (4) How to plan and carry out the anti-prostitution movement. It is heard that after the board of directors determines the plan, it will be submitted to various agencies for implementation. In the final election, Huang Meixian, wife of Niu Yongjian, and Wu Zhiqin, Tao Juying, Liu Jianping, Lu Xifang, Jin Zuoren, and Zhang Bingyue were elected as directors. Pan Shenyan, Sun Shiqing, and Yang Dashi were elected as alternate directors.

Cigarette Lottery Tickets Popular Again in Guangdong Province 170

Shanghai cigarette factories have petitioned the authorities to stop cigarette companies from replacing lottery tickets with empty packs and offering cash prizes. This was very popular in the city last year, but the Ministry of Finance sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Government, which instructed the Social Affairs Bureau and Public Security Bureau to issue a joint ban. At the same time, the Shanghai Cigarette Factory Association held several meetings to discuss the issue, believing that cigarette companies offering prizes was an unfair form of competition that not only did not help sales but also harmed the capital of other companies. They also sent a sincere letter advising them to stop. The Ministry of Finance's Bureau of Unified Taxation also ordered all factories to stop within a time limit and to comply with the following three principles: (1) No lottery tickets may be printed; (2) No cash prizes may be offered; (3) Prizes may not be awarded based on the numbers of officially issued lottery tickets or other tickets. Otherwise, the resident factory officials will be ordered to stop shipping goods. However, recently, the Guangdong province cigarette companies have been replacing lottery tickets with empty packs. It is now heard that various cigarette companies in this city, such as China East and Great East, believe that this not only hinders the promotion of government construction lottery tickets and causes competition among companies but also undermines the authority of the authorities' ban. Therefore, they have jointly petitioned the authorities to ban it immediately to uphold the rule of law.

Aviation Highway Construction Lottery Tickets; Leaflets Distributed by Airplane 171

The National Government's Aviation Highway Construction Lottery Tickets have been issued since May of last year, and five draws have already been held. The credibility is obvious, and sales have increased in each period. The sixth lottery will be drawn on the 29th of this month. It is heard that the China National Aviation Corporation has specially dispatched an aircraft to fly to various ports, such as Shanghai, Zhabei, Nanshi, Nanjing, Jiujiang, Hankou, Yichang, Chongqing, Qingdao, Tianjin, and Beiping, to distribute leaflets to help promote the lottery. This lottery not only increases construction funds for the country but also provides ticket buyers with a limited cost and the opportunity to win a large prize, which is a win-win situation. Therefore, Chinese and foreigners are very enthusiastic about buying tickets.

China Economic Credit Cooperative; Announces First Enlarged Recruitment 172

The China Economic Credit Cooperative held an enlarged recruitment drive for two months starting on the first of this month. The board of directors decided on the 15th of this month to announce the recruitment results every two weeks and set the announcement dates as follows: First time, June 16; Second time, June 30; Third time, July 14; Fourth time, July 31. On the first recruitment on June 16, a total of 125 people were recruited, totaling 63 and one-fifth shares. It is also heard that in addition to the prizes prepared by the cooperative, Chief Captain Zhang Shouzhi donated three large silver shields, honorary chief captain Mayor Wu generously donated a silver cup, honorary deputy chief captain Lin Kanghou donated a large silver cup, honorary deputy chief captain Director Pan Gongzhan donated a large silver cup, and captain Yu Zhongyan donated a silver shield. It is expected that many more prizes will be donated this month to commemorate enthusiastic comrades.

Jardine Matheson & Co.; Trade Situation for Last Year 173

According to the report of the board of directors of Jardine Matheson & Co. Steam Navigation Company, the trade situation for last year was consistently in reverse. The company's transportation business was also largely affected. However, the silver price has improved, so when converting the accounts of various ships from silver dollars to British pounds, it was slightly more favorable. The average ratio in 1932 was 1 shilling and 3.75 pence, and the average ratio in 1933 was 1 shilling and 4.25 pence. It was also said that the ship's passenger and cargo income was £27,332 in 1931, £97,208 in 1932, and £29,837 last year.

Famous Soviet Architect Xu De Visits Shanghai 174

Famous Soviet architect Mr. Xu De visited China to inspect school buildings and was warmly welcomed by the Chinese education authorities. Mr. Xu has traveled to Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Hebei, and other provinces and has made many plans for school buildings in China. He has now completed his inspection and is accompanied by Mr. Li Zongxiang, a specialist from the Ministry of Education, to Shanghai. It is heard that Mr. Xu will return to his country soon.

Wang Zhentao Killed for Selling Inferior Goods; Principal Offender Wang Zhaocheng Arrested; Wang Zhaocheng Claims He Was in Nanjing When the Incident Occurred; Requests Bail, Opposed by Police Lawyer 175

At 9:50 AM on November 18 of the previous year, Wang Zhentao, the owner of Maotai Foreign Goods Store at 310 Xinzha Road, was shot and killed by the Iron-Blooded Punish Traitors Group for selling inferior goods. The police arrested the suspects Pan Hongsheng and four others and handed them over to the First Special District Court. They were found guilty and sentenced to imprisonment. At 11:45 AM the day before yesterday, Ma Bingzhang, a detective from the Jiaxing Road police station, received a report from a triple-light (a reference to a reliable informant) that Wang Zhaocheng, the leader of the case from Haiyan, 42 years old, was hiding at 75 Anyi Village, Lane 74, North Xizang Road. He reported to the police chief and coordinated with Western detectives to go to the address and arrest him. He was taken to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, he was handed over to the Third Criminal Court. The public works bureau lawyer Li Zhishan stated the course of events and said that the defendant denied the case at the police station. He requested a postponement for further investigation and filed a public prosecution based on the crime of murder under Article 282 of the Criminal Law. Wang Zhaocheng testified that he was in Nanjing on business at the time and had nothing to do with the shooting of Wang Zhentao. He had met Pan Hongsheng when he was in the volunteer army and hired lawyers Jiang Yiping and Jiang Chiping to defend him, requesting bail. Lawyer Li said that the case was serious and the police could not agree. Judge Wu Zehan ordered him to remain in custody and adjourned the hearing.

Luo Zhaoxin Assassinated Last Night; Shot in the Back of the Head, Dies in Hospital; Police Investigating the Cause of Death 176

At 8:50 PM last night, a gunshot suddenly rang out in Qinghefang Lane, Zhejiang Road and North Hai Road. Neighbors who heard the sound went out to see that a man wearing a gray serge long gown, with a blue striped silk shirt and pants underneath, and black leather shoes, about 40 years old, was lying on the ground at the back door of the noodle shop in the lane, shot in the back of the head, bleeding profusely, and barely breathing. Nearby patrolmen arrived and immediately reported to the police station. When the Chinese and foreign detectives arrived, the victim was recognized as Luo Zhaoxin (46 years old, from Zhejiang), a lawyer residing at 7 Qinghefang Lane. He was immediately taken to Renji Hospital but died at 9:30 PM due to the severity of his injuries. The body was immediately taken to the morgue for examination and to be reported to the court for inspection. The police are conducting a thorough investigation into the cause of death.

Those present included Zhang Yichen, Wei Langxuan, Ye Qichang, Cai Qiajun, Chen Weiwen, Zhang Yumen, Ren Nongxuan, Liu Zhongying, Zhu Zhichun, Zhou Fuzhang, Chen Jicheng, Cao Zhigong, Chen Jiufeng, Chen Binghui, Wang Hesong, and others.
