Free Talk

Spider 248

— Da Nian

Bats are common in China and are widely liked by the public. They are a symbol of "good fortune," probably because of the similar sound. Occasionally, at dusk, a bat flies into the birdcage, "stopping at the corner of the seat, looking very leisurely." "Unable to speak, please respond with speculation," it is actually a philosophical bat. Is it a bird or a beast? Birds and beasts cannot be in the same group, so let it fly away, whether it is a bird or a beast. But occasionally, in a cool place, a large web is spread, waiting for flying insects. That is the spider.

For a moment, I forgot whether "ju xiao in the house" refers to this creature. In any case, this creature is disgusting because it weaves nets to kill flying insects and also hinders humans. Children often like to hold bamboo branches to break it and drive it away.

In the past, someone discussed the five virtues of chickens, and later a teacher added two more virtues: one is the ability to kill, and the other is the ability to eat. But spiders also have several virtues. Full of knowledge and skill in crafting nets: wisdom. Standing against the wind, unafraid of wind and dust: courage. Being the same color as its surroundings, leaving no trace: harmony. Using stillness to control movement, sitting upright in the center: the Way. Accepting fate and waiting for the right time, being a disciple of Heaven: nourishment. Fleeing into the void with the slightest reliance: concession. Leaving gaps between the lines: benevolence.

Thinking carefully about human affairs, they are no different from this. There are railway networks on the ground, and power grids during wartime. Even everyone has a kind of atmosphere around them, spreading a kind of weaving. Whether it is for fame or for profit, it must make people see through it, and this is the goodness of ethics. In this way, they obtain food and avoid starving. Those with great abilities spread large webs, obtain great peace, and become large spiders; those with little strength only spread small threads and obtain small snacks. Education, etc., is just teaching people how to do it cleverly. Of course, laziness is not allowed, and that is why people are taught to be diligent. One cannot be too exposed, touching the eyes, and that is why people are taught to be humble, self-deprecating, and cultivated.

All worldly affairs are generally like this. This is not sarcasm. Humans are, after all, a kind of animal in nature, with the virtues of nature. The ancients called nature "Heaven," and one should "observe the Way of Heaven and practice the actions of Heaven." But Zhuangzi is unreachable. He tells people to "enter and play in its fence without harming its name," which means turning into a moth and flying through the gaps without touching the threads. However, there is still no philosophy that destroys this network.

Horizontal Mastery 249

— Zhou Muzhai

The word "mastery" is probably used in the Confucian world, with "master of all things" being a compliment and "not mastering all things" being a pejorative. Not mastering is just a single-minded person. Therefore, what scholars devote themselves to is mastering. The meaning of "master of all things" is very vague. Generally, people intentionally or unintentionally tacitly acknowledge Wang Chong's interpretation in "Lunheng": "Those who are well-read in ancient and modern times are masters of all things." In fact, this definition is not complete. Zhang Xuecheng, in his "General Meaning of Literary History," Volume 4, "Horizontal Mastery," said: "The name 'master of all things' cannot be generalized. There is specialization, and there is broad knowledge. Each has its own irreplaceable quality. Each has its own lack of communication, but if there's communication then there will not be benefits. The name 'mastery' is likened to roads that extend in all directions and reach everywhere. It also refers to the knowledge in one's heart. Though there are differences in high, low, partial, complete, large, small, broad, and narrow, all can reach the Great Way, so it is called 'mastery.'" This saying is quite precise. Wang Chong's words only point out one side of mastery, which is incomplete. However, there are many cases of those who appear to be masters of all things but are not actually. Therefore, Zhang specially established the term "horizontal mastery" in addition to "mastery" to include this type of situation. What is horizontal mastery? He continued from the above: "There are also those that cannot extend in all directions and cannot reach the Great Way, but must also be called 'mastery.' This is called 'horizontal mastery.' Horizontal mastery and 'master of all things' are the same and different, close and far, united and separated." This distinction is especially insightful. There are truly countless people in the world who regard horizontal mastery as "mastery of all things" and those who regard themselves as masters of all things through horizontal mastery. Taking Zhang himself as an example, his masterpiece "General Meaning of Literary History" includes the statement "All Six Classics are History." In the "Yi Jiao" chapter, regarding the interpretation of "Zhou Yi" as history, Hu Shi said that it "very much reveals traces of forced connection" (see "Chronicle of Mr. Zhang Shizhai's Life"). However, merely interpreting something as not being perfectly good does not detract from the value of his statement "All Six Classics are History." The so-called "forced connection," in Zhang's own words, falls into the trap of horizontal mastery. Zhang devoted his life to mastery, but even so, there were still places where he could not completely avoid horizontal mastery, which shows that mastery is not easy.

In the past, when people read books, they often spoke of "suddenly becoming thoroughly enlightened." Later generations, upon seeing these words, often thought of this as a miracle. This is because the reader only sees and pays attention to the words "suddenly," but actually does not see and does not pay attention to the words "suddenly." Suddenly becoming thoroughly enlightened is not a miracle. One must know that before this "suddenly," one has already used up a great deal of energy to have this "suddenly" of thorough enlightenment. This is the same principle as the coexistence of gradual change and sudden change. However, today's people seek mastery suddenly. Many books on academic subjects often end with the eye-catching phrase "Master in 100 Days," such as "XX Master in 100 Days." At first glance, it seems to require more effort than "suddenly"; however, the book is only a thin volume, and the time is only 100 days, so it can be calculated that mastery will be achieved. This is indeed a miracle. Although it is said that scientific methods can save human energy, they do not teach people not to learn. Moreover, whether the content of the so-called "Master in 100 Days" leads to mastery or not is still a major question! The term itself is already illogical, and using this term is even more of a distortion. As the saying goes, "Without learning, there is no skill," but now it is "Skill without learning," using skill to drive people into the path of not learning. Here, we do not say "having skill without learning," but "skill without learning" to show that this skill is also very suspicious.

Since recent times, due to the complexity of international relations, there have also been so-called "XX Masters" appearing in droves. This is originally a good phenomenon. But it may not be possible to generalize. Zhang said in the "Horizontal Mastery" chapter that those booksellers, book collectors, and book engravers have said, "These people are nothing more than lute players and tablet craftsmen, whose professions are connected to literature. Since they have contacted many celebrities, they are accustomed to hearing pure words and famous theories. But with no wisdom in their hearts, they hear and tell, and the shallowness of their foundations is not difficult to see." Are not a few words of "Pidgin English" from a foreign language suddenly pleasant to the ear?

In today's atmosphere of floating, shallowness, and shallowness in learning, horizontal mastery is prevalent.

Farm Woman 250

— Lü Shaoguang

She is busy cooking in the kitchen,

Her thin, yellow face flashes with a warm red glow;

But her mind is calculating:

The vegetables in the garden will need manure tomorrow.

The little black dog outside the wooden door

Barks incessantly,

The anxiety of poverty surges to her brow;

Alas, perhaps the grain collector is coming again!

Dang...dang...dang...

A blind fortune-teller

Slowly walks along the muddy path in front of the door.

Feeling something, she sighs with relief, "Ah, bad luck!"

The hen in the yard clucks at dusk.

With a yearning heart, she leans against the wooden door,

In the evening breeze, a shivering voice rises:

"Mom, is Dad back yet? The firewood I chopped today is so heavy!"

Drum Music – One of the Boat Cabin Sketches – 251

— Feng Zikai

I had already decided that I would not go ashore tonight to see the lanterns. I planned to stay in the boat cabin, tidying up the day's drawings under the candlelight at my small table, or lying down to read the newly arrived magazines. When I felt hungry in the evening, I would borrow a bowl from the boat owner's wife and go ashore to buy a bowl of "lifesaving dumplings" to eat. That would be more enjoyable than throwing myself into the whirlpool of the crowd to see the lanterns. But in the end, I changed my mind and went ashore with the boat owner to see the lanterns.

The reason for my change of heart was partly due to the boat owner's encouragement, and partly due to the temptation of the drum music. The boat owner said that tonight's lanterns would be much better than last night's, with decorated platforms borrowed from other docks and a "Jinhua Old Dragon" with over seventy segments. Many people had specially hired boats from afar to see it, so since we happened to be here, we might as well enjoy the spectacle. Hearing about this grand occasion, I felt I should join in the fun. At the same time, the sound of drums and music floated into my boat cabin from all directions, making my feet itch. Involuntarily, I packed up my drawing tools and books and jumped ashore with the boat owner to "share the joy with everyone."

The instruments used in the drum music are all percussion instruments that cannot play melodies. The music played is only a simple repetition of a few tunes, just like the songs children sing: "Dong dong shang, deng deng shang, deng deng ci deng ci deng shang..." But it has a magical appeal that can attract people from far and near. Recalling the sounds of silk strings, bamboo pipes, and wind instruments I heard at the lantern festival last night, although they seemed complex on the surface, in my opinion (actually, listening, but one might as well say seeing) they were simpler than the drum music. Based on my memory, the melodies of the silk strings, bamboo pipes, and wind instruments I heard last night, if recorded in simplified notation, would be nothing more than

51615丨516156丨6161152丨323232

3312丨1611653丨5┆┆

embellishments. Listening to it for too long made my heart itch, which was very unbearable. Moreover, this itch could not be scratched; even if I immediately covered my ears and walked away, I would still carry this itch with me. Drum music is different. When you hear it from afar, your feet itch; as long as you run with the crowd, you will feel refreshed. When you run closer, your body and mind will assimilate into the rhythm of the drum music, and you will become excited with it. Listening to it for too long will at most make you tired, but it will never make you feel unbearable. This is a unique product of Chinese music. As far as I know, Western music does not seem to have any performance method composed entirely of percussion instruments.

Therefore, I went ashore with the boat owner, ostensibly to see the lanterns, but in reality, I wanted to see the performance of the drum music. We stood by the bridge to watch the lanterns. Many lanterns, like sedan chairs, were carried across the bridge. Later, due to obstacles ahead, they all stopped. Standing in front of me was a splendid decorated platform bearing large plaques with the words "Promote Life" and "Share Joy with the People." Behind it was a band of percussionists. I squeezed through the crowd to the back to watch the percussionists' performance closely. The playing method was very straightforward, but the alternating strikes of gongs, drums, cymbals, and other instruments created a kind of graceful and majestic rhythm. The playing of the drums was particularly straightforward, always beating "Dong, dong, dong, dong" without ever changing the rhythm. But because of the cooperation of other instruments, it could express a special effect. The appearance of the drum beater was even more surprising to me: a child was carrying a drum on his back and running forward, while the drummer followed behind, beating the drum all the way, as if chasing a defeated general. The faster the child ran, the tighter the drumming behind him chased. When the child stopped to let him beat, he would take a stance and beat him hard. The child endured the beating on his back while eating a sesame cake in front. The sesame seeds on the cake fell off one after another with the "Dong, dong, dong, dong" of the drum. He reached out and caught the sesame seeds, slowly licking them with his tongue. I went closer to look and saw that his whole body, muscles, and even his hair, were trembling with the beating of the drum. His internal organs must have been vibrating with the sound of the drum. This was an all-encompassing full-body exercise. The sesame cake was probably digested quickly. But looking closely at the child's age, he was only about ten years old. His skin and flesh were very tender, and his bones must not be very strong. Such intense drumming until midnight, his tender bones could be knocked apart, and he would have to go home and have his mother reassemble them.

I quickly took out my sketchbook to capture this amazing scene. After drawing it, the drum band set off and gradually moved away. After putting away my sketchbook and listening to the drum music again, the rhythm was not as graceful and majestic as before, and seemed to carry a hint of sadness. (May 20, 1934)

New Life Movement Lantern Parade

Gui Ying's Father (5) 252

— Hua Zi

"Mr. Xu, my Xiaoyu is smart. He knows I hate the revolutionaries the most, so he hid it from me, hid it from me. At one time, I only saw him very busy, with many people coming and going, sometimes not even returning home all night. At that time, he was teaching at a school during the day, and he still brought his monthly salary home without missing a penny, not like he was gambling or whoring outside, so I didn't bother him. Only my old woman would often scold him, but he didn't say a word. He was very filial. After a few months, one day, Xiaoyu came home and said to me very happily: 'Dad, the National Revolutionary Army has reached Shanghai, and the county party headquarters has been openly established. I have been elected as a formal executive committee member.' I only heard the two words 'revolution,' and I asked, 'What about the revolutionaries? Have they been defeated by the true emperor? What about you?' Later, Xiaoyu explained to me in detail, and I understood what was going on. I knew that the revolutionaries of the past were overthrowing the emperor, and the revolutionaries of today were helping the poor. Now, these revolutionaries who help the poor have won the world, and my Xiaoyu has become the leader of the revolution.

At first, I couldn't help but have some doubts and worries, but that night, I was so happy that I couldn't stand it. That night, many of Xiaoyu's friends came to my house. My house was so small and narrow, like a pigsty, but those friends didn't care. Many people crowded around and discussed things with Xiaoyu. I heard them say that the county magistrate had run away, and now they were discussing who should be the new magistrate. Some people advocated for the scholar Ke, and some advocated for Mr. Zhuang Si, but my Xiaoyu said that they were all old gentry and not revolutionaries. He advocated for Chen Shiyi, the principal of the county high school, to be the new magistrate, and everyone agreed. I admired my Xiaoyu so much. He could actually appoint a magistrate, so wouldn't he be even bigger than the magistrate?

Commentary

A Word for the City's Hygiene Movement 253

— Shou Zi

Hygiene movement is very necessary in our country today. Chinese people are indeed too unhygienic. Foreigners criticize us Chinese in this way, and we ourselves often blame ourselves in this way. However, why are Chinese people so unhygienic? This is another big problem. Chinese people have not always been so unhygienic. It is just that the current China is unable to pay attention to hygiene. How do I mean this? Well, let's see: how many Chinese people can live their extremely ordinary lives safely? Even a meal of rice and porridge is a problem. I ask, in this situation, who has the time and money to pay attention to hygiene? Of course, paying attention to hygiene does not necessarily require much effort or a lot of money. However, in reality, paying attention to hygiene does require considerable effort and money. For example, getting a haircut and taking a bath are very simple hygiene practices. For people with relatively affluent lives, it is not a problem. However, for the vast majority of poor people, it becomes a problem. Getting a haircut costs money, and taking a bath costs money. Although the money is not much, it is still needed. They usually have trouble eating a meal, so they save where they can. Therefore, they can only extend the time between haircuts and baths. This is why they cannot pay attention to this aspect of hygiene. This is still a small problem. There are many other aspects of hygiene that they cannot practice, especially the cleanliness of their homes, daily lives, and diets. They cannot even talk about that. As for getting sick, the problem is even more difficult. They simply have to wait to die, because apart from the quack doctors and wandering practitioners who can be hired for a few hundred coins, ordinary doctors are generally beyond their reach. I ask, in this situation, even if you want them to pay attention to hygiene, how can it be possible? Of course, it is not possible.

The city's Health Bureau has now decided to start a city-wide hygiene movement starting on the 19th of this month. This is certainly a very meaningful and commendable event. We hope that everyone can implement it. However, we further hope that they will take further steps, such as cleaning the streets and removing pits and toilets. This is still preliminary work. The most important thing is how to make everyone pay attention to hygiene and have a proper hygienic environment. This is a fundamental social problem, and a simple hygiene movement cannot be effective. However, we still hope that the health authorities can pay close attention to this. The filth and uncleanness of the working-class areas is a commonly recognized fact. How can we make them clean? Of course, this cannot be achieved by sweeping the streets once or spraying disinfectant once. We must first teach them how to maintain hygiene afterwards. This is the fundamental work. In short, we hope that the authorities can think more about the general poor people. Because the poor people are the most unhygienic. Rich people do not need anyone to tell them about hygiene. They already live very hygienic lives. If we ignore the poor people, the hygiene movement will be fruitless. The health authorities should pay attention to this.

Marriage 254

— Fei

Humans, whether male or female, when they reach a certain age, instinctively activate their youthful functions. At that time, it is the initial period of needing sexual comfort. Due to the beginning of sexual needs, they eagerly hope to get married.

Sexual frustration is a common disease among young people. Because of sexual distress, their spirits decline, and they feel that real life is boring and monotonous. In order to adjust the meaning of life, they have to find a life partner. Marriage is the best and most practical way to solve all these problems. Every young person thinks this way. Once they reach puberty, they will uncontrollably yearn for marriage and to form a small family. Indeed, the ideal married life is so beautiful!

How pleasant! Especially when the happy small family life begins, the entire life is filled with vitality and joy.

The small family is a palace of happiness, a gentle land of fairies, and even a sweet paradise. The surrounding environment seems to be in a rose-colored dream, and the masters living here, of course, seem to be drunk on wine.

However, sweet as it may be, drunk as it may be, the heavy pressure of life increases relentlessly on your shoulders, and the instruments of worry lock you in for life!

Marriage is the tomb of love. The process of people in love is wonderful and bright. However, when love reaches a certain level, they hope to get married sooner and start living together sooner. But after living together, it disappoints you, and you feel that the past was empty, with only that blurry memory lingering on the cerebral membrane.

Life is not completely without happiness, but you have to find happiness yourself. Humanity is not completely without pain, but you have to overcome and resolve the pain yourself. However, the so-called pain and the so-called happiness can only be experienced by the person involved. To a third party, it cannot be definitely asserted. Because everyone's perceptions are different, and because of the differences in perception, the resulting effects are also different. For example, in the eyes of others, you are very happy, but in reality, you feel immense pain! You think that your life is extremely painful, but conversely, I have no feeling, as if it is very happy. In short, these are completely different expressions of each person's feelings and interests. Isn't marriage the same?

My friend Mr. Ma and Ms. Xu were united through a beautiful process of love. Recently, I went to visit them and took the opportunity to inquire about Mr. Ma's life after marriage. He only shook his head at me. At the same time, I went to ask Ms. Xu, and she smiled without answering. Here, they gave me a very clear hint that life after marriage is just like this! But I think, in another three or four years, it may be even more tasteless. There will be a large group of children, the family's finances will also expand accordingly, and life will become unstable. Someone once said that a person who gets married is like being sentenced to life imprisonment. Only today have I proven that this statement is indeed not an exaggeration.

However, all in all, marriage can be said to be the happiest moment in a person's life, but it is also the time when the seeds of the most pain begin to sprout. The flowers that bloom in the future will naturally be filled with worries, and the final fruits will also be bittersweet.

I believe that people who have tried married life will definitely express sympathy for this situation.

Starting with High-Heeled Leather Shoes 255

— Bai Rong

By chance, I read a few words of a French scholar quoted in Plekhanov's book, which made me think of women's high-heeled leather shoes and the extravagant decorations of modern times, and gave rise to many feelings. Those words were like this:

"In Seine-et-Marne, wealthy Negro women wear shoes that are so narrow that they cannot be fully put on. Therefore, these women appear special because of their very restrained walking. However, this way of walking is considered extremely seductive."

Because it is considered extremely seductive, they do not hesitate to endure the pain of restricted movement and wear those unsuitable and uncomfortable shoes. This is not only a "special landscape" of the Negro race. Similarly, there is the three-inch golden lotus of ancient China in the distance, and the high-heeled leather shoes that swept the world in recent times.

To mutilate any part of the body and create a deformed state is to be considered the most absurd thing. Many medical scientists have already proven that high heels are harmful. However, the scientists' impartial arguments cannot match the blind worship of the masses. Thus, in the situation of "the city loves height, and all around increase it by a foot," high-heeled leather shoes were led by a few fashionable cities and became the main trend of women's decoration in an era.

In fact, in our view, this phenomenon is somewhat ridiculous. Instead of using a person's feet to walk straight and balanced, they deliberately stand on tiptoes, creating a crooked and unstable posture to win people's praise. This is simply a bit foolish. However, the defenders repeatedly say: "This increases the graceful figure and the slender waist!" Because in the eyes of these people, only high-heeled leather shoes can increase people's beauty. But is beauty truly

Page 18

an absolute standard? As far as I know, aesthetic concepts often change with social psychology, and the basis of social psychology is the entire social foundation and its era. Beauty changes with changes in time and space. The three-inch golden lotus of ancient times has been abandoned by modern people, and the ear-piercing and colorful decorations of Africa can only prevail in their kind of society and region. Now is the era of capitalist decadence. In the cities of this era, people's psychology tends to be sexually indulgent. They demand that women wear high heels, wear expensive ornaments, apply rouge, and wear yellow powder. Their aesthetic standards are gracefulness, slenderness, delicacy, gentleness, and vividness, and further, they want sensuality! The main purpose of these is to suit their own requirements and enjoyment. Therefore, in this kind of society, high-heeled shoes and various luxury goods are "considered extremely seductive" and sweep the era.

In a male-centered society, the degree of oppression of women can be said to reach the extreme. They cannot have their own standards of beauty. Their standards of beauty must be determined by the needs of the surrounding men. They are regarded as decorations or even playthings and exist in this world. Not to mention women under the control of feudal forces, even women with more progressive thoughts often cannot break through this difficult barrier. Is there anything more unfair than this? However, this "unfairness" has become commonplace, from stimulation to indifference, from indifference to forgetting.

New women must awaken. They should know that this is not only a deception, but simply an insult. They will not pretend and lose their own nature because people "consider it extremely seductive." The first step from awakening to reform is to break the shackles from their limbs and remove high-heeled shoes and many unnecessary decorations from their bodies!

Obligatory Advertisement 256

— San Duo

When I was a child, when I read the Legend of the White Snake, I was just like being poisoned by the strange chivalrous legends, I really wanted to go to Leifeng Pagoda to see the real snake appearance of White Maiden and Little Qingqing. Speaking of it, it is really a pity, it is said that when Leifeng Pagoda collapsed, there was a white light flying into the sky, this is naturally the White Maiden showing her holiness, but the people who saw it did not know the whereabouts of this "going". Moreover, there is no Xu Xian officer reborn as a seven-life boy, of course, the White Maiden has no need to repay her kindness and does not know where to go. After many years, the snake and others probably had their mortal hearts moved again, and they actually rode the clouds to the sea. This Dragon Boat Festival in the 23rd year of the Republic of China is even more spectacular. In addition to the dragon boat races in Bansong Garden, the two divine snakes Bai Qing showed their power at noon. Unfortunately, the snakes were still snakes, and they did not transform into the charming and beautiful White Maiden and Little Qingqing. Otherwise, there would definitely be Xu Xian officers who claimed to be the world's seven-life boys and re-enact a story of righteous demons. But it is enough to look at that paragraph of text to get a taste of it. I think there is no shortage of comrades who are obsessed with the Legend of the White Snake, and I dare not keep it secret, so I introduce it to the left;

Yesterday was the abolished calendar Dragon Boat Festival, the two divine snakes Bai Qing enshrined by this association, when they were showing their power at noon, caused the cage shed to be shattered, and tourists were frightened and fled far away, causing great chaos. We have already added spiritual amulets to suppress and stop it, so that there is no danger. However, we deeply apologize to the tourists who were frightened yesterday, and express our gratitude. (Original text copied verbatim, punctuation added arbitrarily.)

Talking About the Role of Trademarks and Signboards 257

— Ming Tang

In the past, stores always had a signboard, while modern new-style stores, companies, or factories all have trademarks. Trademarks and signboards are all business logos that indicate the identity of a store or company, and imply a certain business or product identity. For example, the trademark of the Family Industrial Cooperative's products is a butterfly made up of the five characters "Family Industrial Cooperative," and the trademark of Chen Jiageng Company's products is a Chinese character "中" with a circle added around it. These trademarks are all product logos that indicate the identity of the factory, and are convenient for buyers to identify.

Trademarks play a very important role. In foreign countries, a trademark can often be valued at tens of thousands to hundreds of thousands of dollars. Because the value of this trademark represents the entire product value of the company or factory. Without commodities as a foundation, trademarks cannot occupy an important position in society; at the same time, without trademarks as identification, commodities cannot stand out and be recognized by everyone at first glance. This shows the value of trademarks.

In the past, my country did not have trademarks, but only signboards. Also, because these signboards were mostly not registered, and there were no registration methods at that time, the imitation of signboards was particularly popular in my country. For example, the Daoxiang Village in Suzhou and the Lugao Jian in Shanghai are almost everywhere, which is one example.

Signboards and trademarks are not only prevalent in commerce, but also in other areas. Especially in the literary world, they have become particularly popular in recent years. Someone has written a strange book or done something strange. At this time, such strange books and strange things can also be used as a trademark or signboard. For example, first there is a collection of love letters, then two more collections come. Then the advertisements boast greatly, saying that the first collection has subverted some of humanity, and of course, the second collection is also very good without saying too much. Everyone, go buy it. Another example is that I have previously written strange books such as the History of Sexuality and have been noticed. Now I will write other articles again, at this time I can bring out the previous strange books and call people to pay attention to me again. In this way, there are more outlets for my articles. Of course, booksellers also make extra money. This is the role of a trademark and signboard.

Similarly, many people have become accustomed to using signboards in recent years. For example, a judge who retires and becomes a lawyer must say: "So-and-so previously served as a judge of the so-and-so High Court, and a judge of the so-and-so District Court." The more official titles, the better. What is the purpose? The purpose is to use this as a signboard. Another example is that people who sell calligraphy and paintings must also put on some former Qing Dynasty scholar-officials, or even what kind of officials. In this way, the person's identity will appear particularly high and elegant, and his works (commodities) can be sold more easily. In addition, fortune-telling and fortune-telling will probably use this trick. Fortunately, society is blind, they think that as long as the signboard is hung well, there is no need to worry about the commodity having no outlets. Are the commodities really good?

The buyers don't care.

Signboards and trademarks are not only prevalent in commerce, but also in all aspects. Alas, this society where everything has been commodified!

Fishing Festival 258

— Sha Yan

Dengjia Yaotou, also known as Dengjia Kou, is a region in Shandong Province with a relatively large fish production. It belongs to Zhucheng County. Every year after Grain Rain, it is the beginning of the fishing season. From the beginning of March to May, this period is called the Fishing Festival.

Ten days before the Fishing Festival, fishermen rushed to Dengjia Yaotou to choose a place to build a shed, as a temporary home during the fishing season. About 2,000 sheds are set up every year. At the same time, in addition to the fishermen who specialize in this period, there are also thousands of sheds that specialize in the fishermen's business, such as: food stalls, tea stalls, smoking dens, wine stalls, gambling grounds, theater stalls, rockers, and other small stalls for daily necessities. It can be said that in addition to the larger stores such as the Jingzhuang gold and silver industry that are generally available in the market, it is simply fully equipped. Moreover, in this shed-covered amusement field, there are also divisions into first-class and second-class, which can be said to be the stratification of classes all over the world.

In the past, fishermen could more or less obtain considerable benefits during this period. However, in recent years, due to the increasing bankruptcy of the social economy, the lack of people's purchasing power, the dumping of foreign fish, the harshness of official passes, and the poor fishing gear, which is not enough to compete with foreign fishing boats that invade our territorial waters, these have led to the fishermen increasingly seeing the dead end of their profession. Therefore, the Fishing Festival in this area has not been as lively and prosperous as it used to be in recent years.

"Note:" Dengjia Yaotou is a place name in Zhucheng County, Shandong Province. The area is rich in fish, so the county people mostly call it Dengjia Yao.

Dawn 259

— Shen

The "whistle" has already sounded for the second time. The third time means it's time to enter the factory, so I hurriedly put on my washed blue cloth short jacket from yesterday, picked up my lunch basket, and ran outside. The sunlight was already covering the ground. I strode towards the factory. A "special vehicle" sped past, filled with comrades in blue cloth short jackets, also on their way to work. Then came barefoot, sturdy men, carrying shoulder poles laden with fresh vegetables, heading to the market to sell. A police officer directed the traffic at the intersection. Students in long silk gowns or cheongsams, carrying small briefcases, were hurrying to school. Athletes were practicing long-distance races on the road. These were what I saw along the way, so I wondered, why couldn't I find what I saw the other day when Aunt Lin took me to play on "Great Avenue"—the gentlemen with handlebar mustaches sitting in cars with their plump, fair-skinned wives, the young masters in foreign clothes and the young ladies walking hand in hand, and the little Pekingese dogs in their arms? After thinking for a while, I realized that this dawning of the morning is the sole prize for us laborers who live by our own efforts.

I happily continued on my way, feeling especially joyful today because I knew that the lovely dawn is exclusively ours, belonging to our class. Although I don't have a moment of rest all day long, at this moment I think, my spirit is joyful. Although I am constantly drenched in sweat every day, the price of this sweat is the rice in my bowl. I maintain my life with my own labor. What a glorious life!

When I arrived at the factory gate, the whistle sounded for the third time, and in that instant, I was swallowed inside.

Thoughts on the Women's Art Exhibition 260

— Ms. Feng Wenfeng

Our art association recently held its first exhibition at the Ningbo Native Place Association. The exhibition lasted for three days, and we received over ten thousand visitors. We received very good reviews from the outside, such as Tang Guanyu, Li Qiujun, Yu Danhan, Gu Qingyao, Yang Xueyao, Yang Xuejiu, Bao Yahui, Xu Hui, Huang Yingfen, Pang Zuoyu, Yu Jingzhi, Jiang Yanan, Ding Yunbi, who are already well-known and need no further introduction. There are also many others, such as Yao Xinhua, He Yi, Wei Xinyun, Fan Caixia, Zhu Zhixian, Weng Wenbi, Weng Qingyun, Pan Wei, and Ding Mubing, whose works also sold quite a bit. Deng Bihua's handwritten Diamond Sutra horizontal plaque has a graceful and charming calligraphy style containing strength. If given time, her calligraphy will be immeasurable. The flowers and plants of Lu Zao and Lu Qin are ancient and elegant, and their bone strength and ink charm are all worth introducing.

I hope that in the future, our women will especially enthusiastically purchase and promote art and not give way to men. It is definitely not enough to just study some superficial fashions and decorations to show her beauty. In this era, many women only focus on imported art. For the essence of national art and literature, they seem to regard it as irrelevant. I believe that most modern women and wives, apart from being able to speak fluent English, rarely study China's inherent art. If you ask them where China's art is, I am afraid that nine out of ten of them will not be able to answer.

Mr. Zhang Shutong's Artwork

Amateur Mailbox

Has She Failed You? 261

Editor:

I am twenty-one years old. At nineteen, I was betrothed through a matchmaker to a woman who is illiterate. We were engaged with the promise of lifelong companionship. Later, my family, due to my grandmother's frequent illnesses, wanted her to live with us to serve soup and medicine. Both parties agreed, so she moved in with my family. Afterwards, when I returned home from work, I taught her to read every day. Therefore, we were quite affectionate and had frequent opportunities to be close. Soon, we had a physical relationship. After it happened, I discovered that she... After we both spoke clearly, it turned out as I had expected. When she was fifteen years old, she had already had sexual relations with a man, about four or five times. But I am a pure virgin and have never had contact with a woman. She is no longer a virgin. How can she face me? So today, I am writing this incoherent letter to my dear editor, asking you to give me a satisfactory answer, okay? I would like to ask you to answer the following questions:

(1) She has already had relations with a man before. If I separate from her now, will I be guilty in the eyes of the law? (However, I have now had three contacts with her.)

(2) Suppose both parties do not divorce, will there be a good result?

(3) She is now a seventeen-year-old woman. Since I have lost my virginity to her, will it hinder my future?

(4) Should I file a lawsuit now? Or what other method should I use to deal with her?

Please give me a thorough instruction that will prevent me from suffering any mental stimulation. Sincerely, Lv Xinqi

Answer: Both men and women should maintain absolute chastity in engagement or marriage and must not have sexual relations with others. But before that, the other party has no right to ask about whether either party has had sexual relations with others and should not pursue it. In other words, chastity does not go back to the past, it only starts after the two are combined. This is the generally recognized concept of chastity today. You think she has failed you because your wife has had sexual relations with others before, which clearly shows that you are still too deeply influenced by the traditional concept of chastity. This is very inappropriate. Of course, we also admit that young men and women should not have sexual relations with others before they are engaged. But this only refers to his personal conduct and chastity. He does not bear the responsibility of chastity for his future spouse. So your wife, if she had sexual relations with others before she was engaged, you have no right to blame her at all. You feel a little regretful because you are a virgin and feel like you have lost your virginity to a woman who is not a virgin. It's funny to say she has failed you, and it's even more incomprehensible to use it as a reason for divorce. I respect you very much for maintaining your chastity before marriage, but may I ask, who doesn't have spring feelings during youth? During this period, if you were tempted by a woman and could not restrain yourself and had sexual relations with her, although this behavior is said to be inappropriate, do you think it should be forgiven? If you were blamed, would you feel that it was not harsh and be convinced? Why did your wife move in to live with you, because "the two were very affectionate, often had opportunities to contact each other, and soon had a physical relationship"? If you think calmly and put yourself in her shoes, I am afraid you will realize that your blaming her is too selfish and narrow-minded. You will laugh at yourself. Your prejudice cannot be used as a reason for divorce, so as long as it exists, you will be in pain and trouble. This is really asking for trouble. On the contrary, if you completely abandon this prejudice and completely forgive her, then she will definitely love you even more, and your "the two are very affectionate" will become "even more affectionate." Wouldn't life be very happy? The happiness of marriage requires the strength of both parties' love. If you marry a woman who was very chaste before, but there is no love between the husband and wife, this is what you can't say. So I hope you don't create trouble for yourself and ruin the relationship between the two, thereby ruining your very happy life.

As for the four questions you asked, they should not have happened, so I won't... Editor

Chastity Memorial Arch (6) 262

— Ling He

"No, you have to know that it was Shimin who wanted me to knock it for him. I was just knocking it down for him, it wasn't what I wanted myself." That child retorted, "To be honest, you go tell his dad, I'm not afraid of him. Just because someone from their own family wants it, am I at fault for knocking it down for them?"

"Huh?" Gray Chicken Woman turned to Shimin and said, "Did you tell him to knock it for you? Be careful your dad beats you to death when you get back. But you're bigger than him," she pointed at that child again, "If he wants it, you just knock it down for him? Why didn't you tell him that it couldn't be knocked down?"

"..." That child didn't say anything, and ran away with the original group of children, leaving his harvesters to return together.

As he was just entering the gate, he first saw his mother drying clothes in the courtyard. His mother saw him, and shouted loudly:

"Where did you run off to? Why did you sneak out early in the morning, making me search everywhere? You really worried me to death. Why didn't you tell me when you were going out? You're so young, running around outside, what if a con man tricked you? Later, I heard someone say that they saw you and Gray Chicken Brother go together, which put my mind at ease."

After a while, his aunt also came. Seeing that his body was covered with rounded mud balls, she knew that he had been catching crickets, so she went to get him a cricket cage and carefully placed them into the cages one by one. Soon, he heard his mother saying again:

"Come on, come eat porridge with me. You didn't eat all morning, you must be starving to death. And your braid isn't combed, looking so disheveled, aren't you upset?"

Shimin didn't want to go. He had caught so many crickets, and he immediately wanted to fight Aunt's Big-Headed Ghost once, to see who was better. But his mother definitely wouldn't allow it, and definitely would drag him to the kitchen. After washing his face, eating porridge, and combing his braid, and changing his shoes that were soaked by the dew, it took half a day to get him all tidied up before he could run away from his mother's side.

First and foremost, he took rice grains to feed the crickets, knowing that they must be very hungry, having not eaten anything all morning. He also ran to the vegetable garden to pick a few loofah flowers, and wanted the ones that still had dew on them. But it was already late, and the dew on the flowers had already been dried by the sun. There was no way, so he had to pick a few and soak them in clear water for a while, so that the flowers had a few drops of water on them, and just let them eat it...So he put the rice grains and loofah flowers into the cage, watching those crickets eating ravenously, almost able to hear the sound of them eating...

A Feud Between Chevalier and MacDonald? 263

— Mei Sheng

Chevalier Denies First, MacDonald Clarifies Later

The feud between Maurice Chevalier and Jeanette MacDonald has been rumored for a long time. The starting point, it is said, was because MGM asked Chevalier and MacDonald to collaborate again on "The Merry Widow," but Chevalier refused the suggestion. They say Chevalier refused because he didn't want to work with Jeanette again, because if he collaborated with Jeanette, her performance would definitely overshadow his. That would be too disadvantageous for him. This rumor has caused a lot of discussion in Hollywood. Later, Chevalier made a statement denying that he had refused to work with Jeanette. But despite the denial, the rumors continued unabated. One journalist specifically asked Jeanette about this matter again. Here is Jeanette's opinion on the matter.

"That's just ridiculous," Jeanette said. "How can they fabricate such rumors? You must think that there's another major dispute between two passionate stars, that they refused to cooperate with each other. In fact, where did the dispute come from? It's all nonsense! The journalist asked again, "Then what do you think of the rumors outside?" Jeanette said directly and frankly: "What else can I think, since there is no such thing? Maurice and I are now, and always have been, very good friends. There has absolutely never been any dispute between us. When I filmed with Chevalier, I never felt any ego in my heart. What else is there to say?" As she spoke, she tucked her jade fingers into her loose, curly, golden hair and combed it. She was still wearing a blue satin nightgown, which was truly charming. After a while, she continued: "Since I was a child, my mother always taught me not to participate in or be involved in any whirlpool of disputes. She said the best way is to not pay attention to that kind of dispute. My mother can set an example in this regard, carefully avoiding all neighborhood disputes and not participating in any opinions. This is a good lesson I learned from my mother, and in this matter, I especially want to listen to her instructions.

"At first, the rumors outside frightened me. Like a hurricane, spinning around me, I was completely a passive subject. But now it's good, Maurice himself came out to deny it, and I am actually the "Merry Widow", what else do I have to say, wouldn't it be creating another anticlimax? What I can say now is that I have been assigned the role of "The Merry Widow", and I am very happy. I know that my collaboration with Maurice will definitely make "The Merry Widow" a perfect work. But one thing I completely agree with Maurice's view is that Maurice and I are not inseparable old partners. We have starred in three films together before, namely "The Love Parade", "One Hour With You", and "Love Me Tonight." But everyone always thinks that we have starred in dozens of films together. In fact, Maurice has starred in many good films alone, and I have starred in many good films alone. However, when we cooperate, plus Ernst Lubitsch as the director, because Mr. Lubitsch is a genius director, it is bound to be successful. Now "The Merry Widow" stars Maurice and I, directed by Ernst Lubitsch, so we have high hopes for this film."

"Some people say that Chevalier is a little jealous of your success, do you believe it?" The journalist asked again. Jeanette said without thinking: "That's all nonsense. In "The Merry Widow", the two roles are at least equally important. Furthermore, Maurice himself is a very recognized artist, why would he want to film me stealing his show? Furthermore, I know very well that Maurice pays great attention to the entire structure of a film. He would never plan for himself and sacrifice the entire film, or adopt a second-rate role as his co-star for the sake of his own performance. I know Maurice very well, how can I believe the rumors outside? Since I don't believe it, what opinions can I express?"

It is found that "The Merry Widow" was filmed once before in 1903. Who the starring actor was, I can't remember for the moment. Now that Jeanette MacDonald and Chevalier are co-starring, of course, it will not be inferior to the previous works. This kind of remake of old movies, such as "White Sister", is also an example. Although it is due to the lack of subject matter, on the other hand, they can also allow us to review the past and learn new things, and will never make us feel bored.

Film Review

Review of "Let's Fall in Love" 264

— Ling He

LET'S FALL IN LOVE

| Great Light

From many films that mainly depict the inside story of the film industry, we can learn a lot about Hollywood, from the process of making films to their own exposure. Originally, this phenomenon was that film merchants sold themselves at all costs in order to cater to the curious interests of movie fans. This is a concrete manifestation of the commercialization of American films.

Now there is another similar story here. We might as well narrate it again.

A certain film company has a Swedish female star. She is very proud and looks down on everything. When she is filming, she refuses to let visitors stay on the set. She is not easy to cooperate with the director or co-stars she does not like. Therefore, when she is about to start filming a new film, she angrily leaves the set and goes home. There is no way but to find another actress who can replace her. Sure enough, the director found a new talent in the circus. In order to gain the trust of the producer and cater to the curiosity of the audience, he used various methods to say that the girl was also Swedish and that her acting skills were very good. Naturally, the producer allocated huge sums of money for publicity, and her reputation became overwhelming. Under such circumstances, the girl felt grateful to the director for his understanding and secretly fell in love with him. Who knew that it would arouse the jealousy of the director's fiancée, who publicly revealed their secret, and they were greatly embarrassed. But because of this excellent publicity material, the film was greatly noticed by the cinemas, who competed to purchase it. In this way, it stabilized the position of the director and the protagonist, and made them unite.

Needless to say, the story itself has no positive nature at all. At most, it is just an ordinary structure. However, if we understand that it is alluding to a certain event, it can bring a sense of lightheartedness to people. This is the success of this film's curiosity, and it is also the business success of the producer. Isn't it so? That proud Swedish star is very similar to the Greta Garbo that people have advertised. As for the creation of another fake Swedish star, we don't need to know what it alludes to, but that Jewish producer is being ridiculed enough.

From this aspect, we can see that the director not only wants the figure and movements of the person who plays Garbo to be similar, but also tries to imitate the pronunciation. Later, he did not use satirical techniques for the fake Swedish star and the director, making the audience seem to sympathize with them. This point is unknown, but the producer is doing his best to satirize the producer. The temperament of that businessman is so ridiculous by Gregory Ratoff's skillful performance. Assuming that the RKO's special war film "The Lost Patrol" starring McLaglen is screened at the Grand Shanghai

This film does have a relaxed effect, so naturally it has a lot to do with him.

From these places, we can see the director's full American special style. He uses extremely economical techniques and quickly passes through several processes in a fast tempo. In particular, the part where people see the advertisement for the heroine in the newspaper is very chaotic, which is even more wonderful. Similarly, for the director's fiancée in the play, she is also portrayed in four or five extremely short scenes, while the important scenes in the play are quite well grasped.

Lightness and liveliness are the essence of "Let's Fall in Love", but this is not what the protagonist Edmund Lowe did, but George Givot, who played Marx, was very successful. However, the new actor Ann Sothern did not see any special achievements, but was just mediocre.

Audience Opinions

The "Three Sisters" is Too Tailed to Wagg the Dog 265

— A Ping

The day after The Song of the Fishermen was screened at Jincheng, director Huang Jinhuan's new work "Three Sisters" by Li Pingqian was also screened at the New Light Theater.

That was adapted from Kikuchi Kan's novel "New Pearl". I remember that when I was auditing at Tongwen, our professor (naturally a Japanese) compared Zhang XX with Kikuchi Kan's works because a classmate proposed it, and he (the professor) scolded the novels as being full of commercialism, and simply did not compare to Zhang's capital in China. Although I have not read his "New Pearl", and I do not know whether the "Three Sisters" after "New Pearl" was brought to the screen has undergone considerable changes from the original work? In short, although the Chinese film industry is in an era of script shortages, how can bringing "New Pearl" and other similar works over and calling it after the grand occasion of "Sisters Flowers" be compared?

After the same director Huang Jinhuan's "Golden Valley" was screened, it received higher evaluations from film critics, but that bright tail extinguished the power of the entire play. However, everyone knows that that is something that cannot be helped, so what about the "Three Sisters" now? The transformation of the eldest sister and the personality of the second sister are completely vague. Finally, Hu Die gave a long sermon and Ma Yicang was beaten. At least when the story progressed to this point, it was a time when people were very happy. However, in order to save the second sister's fiancé, the eldest sister, who had just realized her mistake, immediately knelt down to Ma Yicang and even wrote a submission. Although it gave Hu Die more opportunities to perform and the lower-class audience to laugh a few more times, I don't know how director Li explained to the audience who were holding greater hopes than "Golden Valley" about the tail in this tail?

Film Novel

Sea Withered Stone Railing (Registered Nurse) (11) 267

— Extracted from Splendor

After the tragedy of James's suicide, one day, Peng was in the hospital packing her clothes and belongings into a small suitcase. Schuler was standing beside her watching, inevitably feeling a bit reluctant to part. She said, "Honey, I really hate to see you go. We've shared joys and sorrows and overcome difficulties together for several years now." Peng nodded and looked at Schuler, but had nothing to say. She had already considered it very carefully. She would soon be promoted to head nurse of the municipal hospital, but Miss McKenna had recently resigned to become the head nurse of a new hospital. She had contacted Peng, asking her to join her at the new hospital. Peng had agreed, but she wanted to rest first, and then go to a new environment, do new work, meet new people, and live in a new place—hoping she could change her mood. After McKenna and Peng left the municipal hospital, Schuler naturally rose to the position of head nurse. The increased responsibilities and workload could also give her some spiritual comfort. Therefore, Peng was willing to sacrifice the position of head nurse and go to a new place, letting Schuler be the head nurse of the municipal hospital. She and Schuler both understood that this was the best solution. They looked at each other and smiled bravely.

Suddenly the phone rang—Dr. Hightower requested Peng to come. Peng immediately ran to Hightower's office. Hightower was sitting behind his desk, his eyes staring blankly ahead. Peng's footsteps startled him, and he quickly stood up, speaking to her very earnestly, "So, you are leaving us now." Peng nodded, not knowing what to say. Hightower continued, "I'm afraid I should congratulate you." He said these words with great pain in his heart, but strangely enough, Peng shook her head and said, "No need." Hightower asked, "What's wrong? I thought—" "You thought what? Marrying Gregg? No. Hightower—"

His eyes widened, somewhat disbelieving. He had gritted his teeth to invite her here, prepared to say goodbye, watching her go with someone else. But now—it seemed a glimmer of hope had been reborn for him, which truly left him in bewildered surprise. He only heard a very gentle voice saying, "Sometimes, it takes a major change to see the truth of a matter—no, I'm just leaving this place to rest for a while, and then—" She didn't continue, only looking at Hightower.

Hightower's tense nerves suddenly relaxed. The corners of his mouth twitched slightly, and his eyes showed a hint of a smile. He slowly said, "In the canals of Venice, aren't there still gondolas to ride for pleasure?" Peng returned his smile, her first smile in a week. Her face still showed extreme fatigue, but her eyes radiated a new brilliance. She asked with a smile, "Venetian gondolas? That's something I've always wanted to have the chance to ride." Hightower, hearing this, gained even more courage and moved closer to Peng, earnestly saying to her, "Peng, are you telling the truth?" Peng smiled, and then Hightower said in one breath, "Let's abandon this hospital, and we'll go together, to Europe—Paris—Vienna—Rome—" Peng teased him, saying, "A doctor and a nurse, won't people gossip?" Hightower laughed, "How absurd! I forgot again! Peng, my darling, will you marry me?" They suddenly embraced each other, kissing passionately, but their joy was interrupted by the phone. They only heard Hightower say to the phone curtly, "What? Emergency? No one else?" Hightower hung up the phone, calling her to wait a moment as if he could do nothing. But Peng shook her head and said, "I won't wait—I'll help you." So they both got busy again. (The End)
